Yeɛ Yosef sele oliɛma nemɔ kyɛ, “Me ole Yosef; aso me baba tɛ te ase?” Nakoso oliɛma nemɔ angora ye noa ye, ofikyɛ bɛ nwo dwirili bɛ kyɛ banwu ye ɔ. Na Yosef sele oliɛma nemɔ kyɛ, “Mesrɛ ɛmɔ, ɛ́mɔpingye me nwo wa.” Yiti bepingyele ye.
Na osele bɛ kyɛ, “Ɛmɔ aliɛma Yosef bɔ ɛmɔtɔnene ye maa oofitele Misraim ne, ye ole me.
Na afei nnɛmɔma ɛmɔ wora bɔ, yeɛ nnɛma ɛmɔfu bɛ nwo kyɛ ɛmɔtɔnene me maa mmamvitele ɛwa ɔ; ofikyɛ Nyameɛ somane me kyɛ nni ɛmɔ nyunu na nne mmenia ngoa.
Ɛhɔen piri ne wale maen ye anu ɔ, afoɛ nyɔ ɛhe; nakoso waha afoɛ nnu bɔ yeɛ bɛngɔyɔ eboo na banya aleɛ ɔ. Na Nyameɛ somane me maa nnili ɛmɔ nyunu kyɛbɔ ɛmɔ boso ngonua wɔ aseɛ ye aso ɔ, amaa ɛmɔ bosofoɛ pee anya ngoa.
Yiti nna ɛmɔ yeɛ ɛmɔfale me bɛwale wa ɔ, na mmom Nyameɛ ɔ; na wamaa maayɛ Faro foɛtulɛfoɛ panyi, ɔne ye awuro amukoraa so meneɛ, na nza nde Misraim maen mukoraa so hene.
Yiti ɛ́mɔhã bɛ nwo bɛhɔ me baba berɛ beese ye kyɛ, Ɛwa Yosef nwa: Nyameɛ ayɛ me Misraim amukoraa so meneɛ; yiti ma wɔ nwo yɛ nyera na bra me nwo wa.
Ɛkɔɔtena Gosen mbɔtam, ɛkɔtena kopingye me, ɛne wɔ mma ne wɔ nnomaa mɔ, ɔne wɔ mmoaen ne wɔ nandwie mɔ, ɔne wɔ nningyein amukoraa.
Mengɔma hwee ngohia wɔ wɔ berɛ, ofikyɛ ɛhɔen piri ne, waha afoɛ nnu.
Anyɔ a, ɛne w’awuro ama, ɔne bɔ ele ye amukoraa nwo kɔhyere bɛ.” Ɔtoale so sele oliɛma nemɔ kyɛ, “Ɛmɔ nye tua, yeɛ nniɛma Benyamin koso nye tua kyɛ me bɔbɔ deinn yeɛ me ne ɛmɔ yɛdwudwo ye.
Ɛ́mɔhã me diberɛ bɔ nne ye wɔ Misraim ɔne bɔ ɛmɔanwu ye amu behyire me baba.
Ɛ́mɔhã bɛ nwo bɛɛfa me baba bɛbra wa.” Afei ɔto brale oliɛma Benyamin osuni, na Benyamin koso to brale ye suni.
Na ɔfele oliɛma nemɔ amukoraa bɛ noa, na ɔtotɔle bɛ nu suni.
Ye si ye, oliɛma nemɔ ne ye belili ngɔmɔ.
Na Faro awuro ama tele kyɛ, “Yosef aliɛma mɔ awa” nen, ɔyɛle Faro ne ye mbanyi mɔ fɛ paa.
Yeɛ Faro sele Yosef kyɛ, “Ka kyire eliɛma nemɔ kyɛ, ‘Ɛ́mɔwura aleɛ bɛsoasoa ɛmɔ ngaka nemɔ na ɛmɔsa bɛhɔ Kanaan aseɛ so; na ɛmɔɔfa ɛmɔ ase ne ɛmɔ awuro ama mɔ bɛbra me wa.
Na Misraim aseɛ ne, ngɔma ɛmɔ nekaa bɔ ɔte paa paa ɔ, ná ɛmɔanya aseɛ ne aso aleɛ paa bali.’ Na sá hyɛ bɛ kyɛ, ‘Ɛ́mɔfa teaseɛnam mɔ béfi Misraim maen nu na ɛmɔɔfa ɛmɔ mma ne ɛmɔ aye mɔ, na ɛ́mɔfa ɛmɔ ase bɛbra.
Nnɛma ɛmɔdwene ɛmɔ agyapadeɛ bɔ ɔkɔha dɔ nwo, ofikyɛ Misraim aseɛ so nningyein paa amu te ɛmɔ deɛ.’ ” Yisrael mma nemɔ yɔle sɔ.
Yosef mane bɛ teaseɛnam mɔ kyɛbɔ Faro hyɛle ne, na ɔmane bɛ aleɛ bɔ bekoli ye atunu ɔ. Ɔmane ebiala ataadeɛ bɔ ɔyɛ nyemene ko, nakoso Benyamin de, ɔmane ye ɛdwetɛ kɔyɛ kilo nza ne ndaadeɛ nyemene ahoroɔ nnu.
Na ɔfale nningyein hemɔ manene ye baba: afunum nyii buru bɔ bafa Misraim nningyein paa basoa bɛ, afunum mmeleɛ buru bɔ basoa bɛ aburoo, paanoo, ɔne aleɛ bɔ ye baba koli ye atee nu ɔ. Oguale oliɛma nemɔ ate, na besi nu nen, osele bɛ kyɛ, “Nnɛma ɛmɔkɔko atee nu oo.” Yiti befili Misraim, na beedwuli bɛ se Yakob berɛ wɔ Kanaan aseɛ so.
Na bɛbɔle ye amaneɛ kyɛ, “Yosef tɛ te ase, na odi hene wɔ Misraim aseɛ mukoraa so.” Na ye ti anu yɛle ye nnaa, ofikyɛ wanne bɛ wanni.
Nakoso bɛhane bɔ Yosef aha ahyire bɛ ne amu behyirele Yakob.
Na Yakob nwuni teaseɛnam mɔ bɔ Yosef asoma kyɛ bɛfa bɛɛfa ye nen, ye kra wale ye nwo.
Na Yisrael sele kyɛ, “Ɔte nahorɛ, mma Yosef tɛ te ase; ngɔhɔ ngoonwu ye koraka né mawu.”
Yakob ne ye awuro ama kɔ Misraim Yiti Yisrael, bɛ besa bɛfrɛ ye Yakob ne sesale ye nwo nningyein amu, na ɔpene atee so.
Oodwuli Beɛ Hyeba, na ɔbɔle afɔleɛ mane ye baba Yisake Nyameɛ.
Na Nyameɛ dwudwo hyirele Yisrael kɔngɔen ne wɔ nyekyire nu.
Ɔfrɛle ye: “Yakob, Yakob,” na osurole kyɛ, “Me ɛhe.” Na osele kyɛ, “Me ole Nyameɛ, wɔ baba ye Nyameɛ, nnɛsuro kyɛ ɛkɔhɔ Misraim, ofikyɛ ngɔma wɔ bosofoɛ kɔyɛ maen kandinga wɔ dɔ.” Me bɔbɔ me ne wɔ kɔhɔ Misraim, na ngosa ngɔfa wɔ bosofoɛ ngɔwa sɔ aseɛ ye aso; na Yosef yeɛ okogua wɔ noa nu nzue ɔ.” Yakob sili nu fili Beɛ Hyeba.
Na Yisrael mma nemɔ fale bɛ baba, bɛ mma mɔ, ɔne bɛ ye mɔ tenatenane teaseɛnam mɔ bɔ Faro fa somane kyɛ bɛfa bɛɛfa ye nemɔ anu.
Yakob ne ye sasofoɛ amu fale bɛ nyɛmmoa ne bɛ nningyein bɔ benyane ye wɔ Kanaan aseɛ so ne, na bɛwale Misraim.
Ɔne ye mma mmienzua mɔ, yeɛ afei ye mma mmienzua nemɔ bɛ mma mmienzua ne mmrasua, ye mma mmrasua mɔ, ɔne ye sasofoɛ amukoraa yeɛ bɛwale Misraim ɔ. Yisrael sasofoɛ bɔ bɛwale Misraim nemɔ ɛhe: Yakob ne ye mma mɔ.
Yakob bamuɛbaa Ruben, yeɛ afei Ruben mma mɔ: Hanoke, Palu, Hesron ne Karemi.
Simeon mma mmienzua mɔ: Yemuel, Yamin, Ohade, Yakin, Soha yeɛ Sɔɔlo bɔ oni te Kanaanniɛ ne.
Lewi mma mmienzua mɔ: Gɛsɔn, Kohate ne Merari.
Yuda mma mɔ: Ɛre, Onan, Hyela, Pɛrɛse ɔne Sera (nakoso Ɛre ne Onan bewuli wɔ Kanaan aseɛ so).
Pɛrɛse mma mɔ ole Hesron ne Hamul.
Yisaka mma mmienzua mɔ: Tola, Puwa, Yob ne Simron.
Sebulɔn mma mmienzua mɔ: Serede, Elon ne Yaleel.
(Lea mma mmienzua bɔ Yakob ne ye wole wɔ Padan Aram mɔ ɛhe.
Ɔwa brasua ole Dina.
Ye mma ne ye nnomaa mɔ bɛ somaa te aburasa ne nza.)
Gade mma mmienzua mɔ ɛhe: Sifion, Hagyi, Suni, Esebon, Ɛri, Arode ne Areli.
Asɛ mma mmienzua mɔ ɛhe: Yimina, Yisua, Yisuwi, Beria, ɔne b’eliɛma brasua Sera.
Beria mma mmienzua mɔ ɛhe: Heberi ne Malkiɛl.
(Silpa, bɔ Laban fale ye mane ɔwa brasua Lea maa ɔɔyɛle ye afaneɛ ne, ɔne Yakob bɛ mma ne bɛ nnomaa buru ne nzia nemɔ ɛne).
Yakob aye Rahɛl, ye mma mmienzua mɔ ɛhe: Yosef ne Benyamin.
Yosef ne Asenate bɔ ɔte On sɔfo Pɔtifɛra awa brasua ne, bɛwole Manase ne Efraim wɔ Misraim maen nu.
Benyamin mma mmienzua mɔ ɛhe: Bela, Bekya, Asebel, Gera, Naaman, Ehi, Rohye, Mupim, Hupim ne Ade (Rahɛl ne Yakob bɛ mma ne bɛ nnomaa, bɛ mukoraati bɛte buru ne nna).
Dan awa bienzua ɛhe: Husim.
Nafetali mma mɔ ɛhe: Yaseel, Guni, Yesare, ɔne Silem.
(Bilha bɔ Laban fale ye mane ɔwa brasua Rahɛl kyɛ ɔɔyɛ ye afaneɛ ne, ɔne Yakob bɛ mma ne bɛ nnomaa mukoraa te nzoo).
Yakob ye bɔbɔ ye sasofoɛ mukoraa bɔ ɔne bɛ wale Misraim ne, sɛ ɛye ye mma mmienzua nemɔ bɛ ye mɔ esie ahameɛ a, bɛ mukoraa bɛte aburasia ne nzia.
Yosef mma bɔ ɔwole bɛ wɔ Misraim nemɔ te nyɔ; Yakob ne ye awuro ama bɔ bɛwale Misraim ne amukoraa bɛte aburasoo.
Yakob ne ye awuro ama kofite Misraim Yakob somane Yuda maa olili ye nyunu moa hɔle Yosef berɛ kyɛ Yosef ohyire ye Gosen atee, na bɛwale Gosen mbɔtam.
Yosef siesiele ye teaseɛnam na ɔfole ooyiale ye baba Yisrael wɔ Gosen.
Ɔfale ye nwo hyirele ɔse; ɔtɔle ye nu, na ɔfale ye ti tole ye kɔme anwo suni hyɛle paa.
Na Yisrael sele Yosef kyɛ, “Afei de mewu po a, mekuro, ɔnate kyɛ manwu wɔ nyunu, na manwu kyɛ ɛte ase.” Na Yosef sele oliɛma mɔ ne ɔse awuro ama nemɔ kyɛ, “Ngɔhɔ Faro berɛ ngɔɔbɔ ye amaneɛ kyɛ, ‘Nniɛma mɔ ne me baba awuro ama bɔ né bɛwɔ Kanaan aseɛ so ne, bawa me wa.
Bɛte mmoaenneafoɛ, ofikyɛ besie ngaka; na bafa bɛ mmoaen ne bɛ nandwie mɔ ne bɛ nwo nningyein mukoraa bawa wa.’ Sɛ Faro frɛ ɛmɔ na obisa kyɛ, ‘Nzikyɛ adwuma yeɛ ɛmɔyɔ ɔ?’ a, ɛ́mɔbua ye kyɛ, ‘Ofi yɛ ngwadaa nu bɔ ɔbaadwu ɛnɛ ye, wɔ ngoaa mɔ de, yɛte mmoaenneafoɛ kyɛ yɛ nana mɔ ala.’ Sɛ ɔba ye sɔ a, ɔkɔmaa ɛmɔkɔtena Gosen mbɔtam, ofikyɛ Misraimfoɛ kyi mmoaenneafoɛ kɔkɔkɔkɔ.”
Yiti Yosef hɔle ɔɔbɔle Faro amaneɛ kyɛ, “Me baba ne nniɛma mɔ, bɛ ne bɛ mmoaen, bɛ nandwie, ɔne bɛ nningyein mukoraa bafi Kanaan aseɛ so bawa, na kekesaala ye bɛwɔ Gosen mbɔtam.” Yosef yele oliɛma nemɔ anu nnu, na ɔne bɛ hɔle kyɛ beesoma Faro.
Na Faro bisale oliɛma nemɔ kyɛ, “Nzikyɛ adwuma yeɛ ɛmɔyɔ ɔ?” Na bebuale Faro kyɛ, “Wɔ ngoaa mɔ te mmoaenneafoɛ kyɛ yɛ nana mɔ ala.” Bɛtoale so besele Faro kyɛ, “Yawa kyɛ yɛbaatena maen ye anu, ofikyɛ wɔ ngoaa mɔ, yɛnnya aleɛ yɛmma yɛ ngaka mɔ.
Ɛhɔen piri bɔ ɔwɔ Kanaan aseɛ so ne noa yɛ se paa.
Yiti kekesaala ye, yɛsrɛ wɔ, maa wɔ ngoaa mɔ yɛtena Gosen mbɔtam.” Yeɛ Faro sele Yosef kyɛ, “Wɔ baba ne eliɛma mɔ bawa baaboka wɔ so wɔ wa.
Misraim aseɛ ne wura wɔ sa, ma wɔ baba ne eliɛma mɔ bɛtena aseɛ ne nekaa bɔ ɔkye aleɛ paa ɔ. Maa bɛtena Gosen mbɔtam, na sɛ ɛse bɛ nu biemɔ bɔ bɛkɔhora a, maa bɛnea me nyɛmmoa deɛ mɔ bɛma me.” Afei Yosef mane ye baba Yakob wale oosomane Faro, na Yakob yirale Faro.
Na Faro bisale Yakob kyɛ, “Ali afoɛ nyɛɛ?” Yakob buale Faro kyɛ, “Mahyini aseɛ ye aso afoɛ ɛyaa ko ne aburasa; m’afoɛ ne anzo pee, ye somaa ndwu afoɛ bɔ me nana mɔ lili ɔ, nakoso ɛfɛɛ wɔ nu paa.” Yakob yirale Faro, na ofili Faro nyunu berɛ ɔhɔle.
Yeɛ Yosef bɔle ɔse ne oliɛma mɔ atenaseɛ, na ɔmane bɛ aseɛ bɔ ɔkye aleɛ paa wɔ Ramese mbɔtam wɔ Misraim maen nu, kyɛbɔ Faro hyɛle ne.
Na Yosef mane ɔse ne oliɛma mɔ ne ɔse awuro ama mukoraa bɛ noa aleɛ, kyɛbɔ ebiala ye sasofoɛ somaa te ɔ. Ɛhɔen piri ne anu yɛ se Né aleɛ nne aseɛ ne aso nekaa biala; ofikyɛ ɛhɔen piri ne anu yɛle se paa, ɔnate sɔ ati né Misraim maen ne Kanaan maen nu mmenia mukoraa bɛ́teetee.
Né Misraim aseɛ so ne Kanaan aseɛ so sikaa mukoraa waali Yosef berɛ, ɔnate aburoo bɔ bɛtɔle befili ye berɛ ne ati, na Yosef fale esikaa ne hɔle Faro awuro.
Na mmerɛ bɔ Misraimfoɛ ne Kanaanfoɛ bɛ sikaa amu yiele ne, Misraimfoɛ amukoraa wale Yosef berɛ beesele ye kyɛ, “Ma yɛ aleɛ; aso odi kyɛ yɛwuwu wɔ wɔ nyunu wa?
Yɛ sikaa mukoraa ayie.” Yeɛ Yosef sele bɛ kyɛ, “Sɛ ɛmɔ sikaa amu ayie a, nzaade ɛ́mɔfa ɛmɔ nyɛmmoa mɔ bɛbra maa mva nzesã aleɛ mma ɛmɔ.” Yiti bɛfale bɛ nyɛmmoa bɛbrɛle Yosef, na Yosef mane bɛ aleɛ ɔfa sesane bɛ mbɔngɔ mɔ, bɛ mmoaen, bɛ nandwie mɔ ne afunum mɔ.
Ɔmane bɛ aleɛ ɔfa sesane bɛ nyɛmmoa mukoraa sɔ afoɛ ne.
Na sɔ afoɛ ne sone nen, ye afoɛ bieku besa bɛwale ye berɛ beesele ye kyɛ, “Yɛngɔfa ngɔfea me mene kyɛ yɛ sikaa mukoraa ayie, na nandwie nemɔ baali yɛ mene sa nu, na ɛhwee nne berɛ bɔ yɛkɔfa yɛkɔbrɛ me mene ɔ, sana yɛ nipadua ɔne y’aseɛ ala. Nzu ati yeɛ odi kyɛ yɛwuwu wɔ wɔ nyunu wa ma y’aseɛ mɔ ka berɛ ɔ?
Tɔ yɛ ne y’aseɛ ná ma yɛ aleɛ, na yɛkɔyɛ Faro ngoaa, na yɛ aseɛ ayɛ ye deɛ.
Ma yɛ aburoo bɔ yɛkolua ɔ, amaa yanwuwu, na mmom yanya yɛ ti yadidi nu, na aseɛ ne koso wanna berɛ mbaen.” Yiti Yosef tɔle Misraim aseɛ ne amu mane Faro.
Ɔnate ɛhɔen piri bɔ né ɔdosa mmenia ne ati, Misraimfoɛ amukoraa tɔnetɔnene b’aseɛ.
Aseɛ ne ɔɔyɛle Faro deɛ, na mmenia ne de, ofi Misraim sorɔ bɔ ɔkwaadwu ye ngwaen, Yosef maa bɛyɛle Faro ngoaa.
Asɔfo nemɔ aseɛ angome yeɛ wandɔ ɔ; ofikyɛ asɔfo nemɔ de, né Faro tua bɛ kerɛ, na bɛfale sɔ akatuaa ne bɛneane bɛ nwo, yiti bandɔne b’aseɛ deɛ mɔ.
Yiti Yosef sele mmenia nemɔ kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔtie, ɛnɛ kyẽa ye, matɔ ɛmɔ ne ɛmɔ aseɛ mama Faro.
Aburoo bɔ bedua ɛhe.
Ɛ́mɔlua ye wɔ aseɛ ne aso.
Sɛ buberɛ dwu a, ɛmɔkɔhyɛ fieso aleɛ ne anu nnu: ko kɔyɛ Faro deɛ na nna ayɛ ɛmɔ deɛ.
Ɛmɔkolua bie fieso, na ɛmɔ ne ɛmɔ awuro ama ne ɛmɔ mma mɔ bali bie.” Na besele ye kyɛ, “Ale yɛ ngoa, maa me mene ɔpene so, na yɛkɔyɛ Faro ngoaa.” Yiti Yosef hyɛle mmeraa fale Misraim aseɛ nwo, bɔ ɔtɛwɔ berɛ ɔbaadwu ɛnɛ ɔ, kyɛ fieso nningyein biala bɛkyɛ nu kure nnu a, ko te Faro deɛ; asɔfo nemɔ aseɛ ngome yeɛ wanyɛ Faro deɛ ɔ. Yakob nzamanzeɛ Yiti Yisrael tenane Gosen mbɔtam wɔ Misraim maen nu.
Benyane agyapadeɛ wɔ berɛ, na bɛwowole bɛyɛle pee.
Na Yakob tenane Misraim aseɛ so afoɛ buru ne nzoo.
Yiti Yakob lili afoɛ ɛyaa ko ne aburanna ne nzoo.
Na mmerɛ bɔ Yisrael wue pingyele ne, ɔfrɛle ɔwa Yosef sele ye kyɛ, “Sɛ anya alo me a, ye de fa wɔ sa bawura me sɔ abo, na hyɛ ɛbɔ kitii kyɛ ekoli nahorɛ kɔma me: Sɛ mewu a, nnɛsie me wɔ Misraim.
Na mmom maa ngɔnna nekaa bɔ me mbanyi mɔ la ɔ; fa me fi Misraim na kosie me wɔ me mbanyi mɔ asieleɛ.” Na Yosef buale ye kyɛ, “Yoo, ngɔyɔ ye kyɛbɔ aha ne ala.” Yakob toale so kyɛ, “Ta ndaen kyire me.” Na Yosef tale ndaen hyirele ye.
Na Yisrael bɔle ye nu ase fale ye ti kisale mba ne sorɔ.
Yakob yira Efraim ne Manase Na ɛhe asi ne, bɛɛbɔle Yosef amaneɛ kyɛ, “Wɔ baba nde apɔ.” Yiti ɔfale Manase ne Efraim bɔ bɛte ye mma nyɔ ne bokale ye nwo so.
Na ebie sele Yakob kyɛ, “Ɛwa Yosef awa wɔ wa.” Yiti Yisrael kendene ye nwo tenane ye mba ne aso.
Na Yakob sele Yosef kyɛ, “Ɛdangama Nyameɛ yele ye nwo ali hyirele me wɔ Luse bɔ ɔwɔ Kanaan aseɛ so.
Oyirale me, na osele me kyɛ, ‘Ngɔmaa ɛkɔwo na wɔ boso atrɛ; ngɔma wɔ boso ama kɔyɛ mmeni kure pee, na ngɔfa aseɛ he ngɔhyɛ wɔ ne wɔ boso ama afebɔɔ.’ Na afei wɔ mma mmienzua nyɔ nemɔ bɔ ɛwole bɛ wɔ Misraim koraka yeɛ meba wɔ wa wɔ Misraim nen, mekyire Efraim ɔne Manase, bɛte me deɛ; bɛkɔyɛ me mma kyɛbɔ Ruben ne Simeon bɛte ne ala. Ngwadaa bɔ ɛkɔwo bɛ nziɛ ye de, bɛte wɔ deɛ; na sɛ ɔba agyapadeɛ hyɛlɛ nu a, b’eliɛma nemɔ dumaa yeɛ ɔkɔla bɛ deɛ so ɔ. Ofikyɛ mvi Padan méba ne, atee nu, ɔhale kãa maa yɛdwu Efrate ne, Rahɛl wuli Kanaan aseɛ so mane me wora bɔle, na nziele ye wɔ Efrate (bɔ ye ole Betlehem) atee nu.” Na Yisrael nwuni Yosef mma nemɔ nen, obisale kyɛ, “Na nwa mɔ ɛhe?” Yosef buale ye baba kyɛ, “Me mma mɔ bɔ Nyameɛ afa bɛ alo me wɔ wa ɛne.” Na Yakob sele ye kyɛ, “Mesrɛ wɔ, fa bɛ pingye me nwo wa maa nyira bɛ.” Ɔnate enyinɛ ti, né Yisrael nye ayɛ wusiwusi maa onnwu nikye.
Yiti Yosef fale bɛ pingyele ye, na Yisrael fele bɛ noa tɔle bɛ nu.
Yisrael sele Yosef kyɛ, “Mandwene kyɛ ngonwu wɔ nyunu ko le, nakoso nea kyɛ Nyameɛ amaa manwu wɔ mma mɔ koso po ɔ.” Yosef pagyale ngwadaa nemɔ fili Yisrael gya so, na Yosef kunduni fale ye nyunu butuli berɛ.
Na Yosef fale bɛ munyɔ pingyele ɔse.
Ɔfale ye sa famaa sɔle Efraim nu maa oolili Yisrael sa bɛen so, yeɛ ɔfale ye sa bɛen sɔle Manase nu maa oolili Yisrael sa famaa so.
Yisrael tengyɛle ye sa famaa fa tole Efraim bɔ yeɛ ɔte kãa ne ti so, na ɔfale ye sa beale nu fale bɛen ne tole Manase so, ɔwɔ nu kyɛ né Manase yeɛ ɔte bamuɛbaa ɔ de.
Na oyirale Yosef kyɛ, “Nyameɛ bɔ me mbanyi mɔ Abraham ne Yisake bɛsole ye ne, Nyameɛ bɔ wagyina me si me wiase bɔ mmale maa waadwu ɛne ye, abɔfo bɔ aye me afi musue mukoraa nu ɔ, yira mmɛɛmaa ye; maa ɔnate bɛ so, me dumaa, ɔne me mbanyi mɔ Abraham ne Yisake dumaa otira ndii; ma bɛ boso ama bɛsone na bɛyɛ pee wɔ aseɛ ye aso.” Na Yosef nwuni kyɛ ye baba afa ye sa famaa wato Efraim ti so nen, wanyɛ ye fɛ; yiti ɔyele ye baba sa fili Efraim ti so fa tole Manase ti so.
Yeɛ Yosef sele ye baba kyɛ, “Daabi, baba, ɛhe yeɛ ɔte bamuɛbaa ɔ, yiti fa wɔ sa famaa ne to ye ti so.” Nakoso ye baba ambene, na osele kyɛ, “Mese, mma mese, ɛhe koso kɔyɛ maen, ye koso ɔkɔyɛ sona titire, nakoso oliɛma kãa ne koli mu kɔtra ye, na ye bosofoɛ kɔyɛ maen maen pee.” Yiti oyirale bɛ sɔ kyẽa ne, na osele kyɛ, “Ɔnate wɔ so yeɛ maen Yisrael kɔha sɔ saleɛ dwirɛ he ɔ: ‘Nyameɛ ma ɛyɛ kyɛ Efraim, na ɔ́ma ɛyɛ kyɛ Manase.’ ” Yiti Yakob nate sɔ atee he aso bɔle Efraim panyi wɔ Manase so.
Yeɛ Yisrael sele Yosef kyɛ, “Mebaawu, nakoso Nyameɛ kogyina ɛmɔ si, na okosa kɔfa ɛmɔ kɔhɔ ɛmɔ nana mɔ aseɛ so.
Afei koso, aseɛ ko bɔ ɔla bokaa Sɛkem ndoroleɛ nu, bɔ mvale me ngrandɛ ne me agyaen ngo nnele mvili Amorifoɛ sa nu ne, mafa mama wɔ; mamva mamma eliɛma nemɔ.”
Yakob yirayira ye mma mɔ Yakob frɛfrɛle ye mma mɔ, na osele bɛ kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔboaboa ɛmɔ noa ma nga bɔ kyẽa bie okosi ɛmɔ bra nu ɔ ngyire ɛmɔ.
“O Yakob mma, ɛ́mɔyia na ɛ́mɔtie, ɛ́mɔtie ɛmɔ ase Yisrael.
Ruben, wɔ yeɛ ɛte me bamuɛbaa ɔ, m’anwoserɛ, me sɛngyerɛnneɛ bɔ oli moa bɔ okyire kyɛ nde bienzua ɔ, w’anidie tra so, yeɛ wɔ tumi koso tra so.
Ɛwosowoso kyɛ nzue, yiti wɔ panyililɛ ne kɔbɔ wɔ, ofikyɛ ɛne ɛse aye bɛlale; ɛɛlale me bɛen so, eguale ye nwo fiɛ.
Simeon ne Lewi te aliɛmaa, bɛ ngrandɛ mɔ te nzɛmmɔne akodeɛ Ao me kra, nnɛne bɛ fa adwene; Ao me sunzum, nnɛne bɛ bɔ afɛ; ofikyɛ sɛ bɛfɛ yaa a, bedi awue, na bɛgye bɛ nye a, bɛpepɛ nandwie mɔ gya ndii nu.
Musue to b’ɛyaafɛlɛ ne, ofikyɛ ye noa yɛ hye; ɔ́hã b’ɛyaafɛlɛ piri ne koso, ofikyɛ atianuserɛ wɔ nu!
Ngɔhyehyɛ bɛ bosofoɛ nu wɔ Yakob maen ne anu, na mato bɛ mapete Yisrael maen nu.
Yuda, eliɛma mɔ kɔkamvo wɔ, na ɛkɔfo kɔtena wɔ pɔfoɛ mɔ kɔme so; ɛse amma mmienzua mɔ kɔkoto wɔ.
Yuda te gyata akrɔngrɔma, bɔ eku ngaka di ná esa bada wɔ boso ɔ. Okunduni, na obutuli berɛ kyɛ gyata, ɔte kyɛ gyata beleɛ; nwa yeɛ onzuro bɔ okotingye ye ɔ?
Ɛhɔtɔ ngofi Yuda sa nu, yeɛ ahennie pɔmaa ngofi ye gya afia, kɔpem kyɛ mmenia kotua ndɔ bɛkɔma ye ɔ, kɔpem kyɛ maen maen kɔyɛ sotie bɛkɔma ye ɔ. Na ɔkɔmenda ye pɔngɔ akrɔngrɔma kɔbɔ bobe nu, na wamenda ye afunum ba wabɔ bobe paa nu, na ɔpo ye ndaadeɛ wɔ nzaa nu, na wapo ye tena wɔ bobe nzaa bɔ ɔyɛ fɛ nu; Ɔkɔno nzaa somaa biala bɔ okuro ɔ, ná nyɔfonesue ama ye gye ayɛ hyɛnn.
Sebulɔn kɔtena mboanoa, ɔkɔyɛ ɛlɛen mɔ agyinaleɛ, na ɔne Sidon bɛkɔbɔ ɛwɛen.
Yisaka te afunum anwoserɛniɛ, obutu mmoaen kure mɔ afia; na onwuni kyɛ nekaa bɔ bede bɛ nwome te paa, na sɔ aseɛ ne yɛ nyemene, yiti ɔhane ye bati ase fa soale nningyein ne, na bɛhyɛle ye maa ɔyɛle kanganiɛ adwuma.
Dan kobua ye mmenia ndɛen, kyɛbɔ Yisrael mmusua kure ngaa nemɔ yɔ ne ala. Dan kɔyɛ atunu ewoo, na wayɛ atimbire so ɛbɔnaa, bɔ ɔkeka pɔngɔ gya ndii nu ɔ, maa pɔngɔhanɛniɛ ne ɔte tɔ ye si ɔ. Ao AWURADE, wɔ ngoalelɛ yeɛ menea ye ate ɔ. Apaabɔlɛfoɛ kure kohwi kɔfa Gade so, nakoso ɔkɔkakyi ye nwo kɔbɔ bɛ so apaa.
Asɛ aleɛ kɔyɛ bɔ ɔte aleɛ paa ɔ, na ɔkɔma mmenia sa kɔha aleɛ bɔ ɔfata ɛhene mɔ ɔ. Nafetali te wanzane beleɛ bɔ basangye ye ɔ, bɔ ofifi mmɛen nyemene ɔ. Yosef te bakaa mmaen frɔmfrɔm bɔ osu ɔ, bakaa mmaen frɔmfrɔm bɔ osu ná opingye asue ti ɔ; ye mmaen bua kogua fasue so.
Agyaentolɛfoɛ dwɔsole tiale ye serɛserɛ, bɛfale agyaen bɛneane ye so bɛtole, na bɛtanene ye nye paa; nakoso wando ye agyaen ne, Ɔnate Yakob ye Tuminiɛ ne ye anwoserɛ ti, ye abasa nu kɔyɛ se.
(Ɔnate Mmoaenneafoɛ bɔ yeɛ ɔte Yisrael Nyɔbotaen ne dumaa nu).
Wɔ baba ye Nyameɛ yeɛ ɔkɔboka wɔ ɔ, Ɛdangama Nyameɛ yeɛ okoyira wɔ ɔ, ɔkɔfa nyameɛso anwuro anwuro saleɛ yeɛ okoyira wɔ ɔ; aseɛ bo dɔ saleɛ buma bɔ ɔtrɛ ɔ, nyɔfone ne aworɛ nu saleɛ yeɛ ɔkɔfa koyira wɔ ɔ. Saleɛ bɔ ofi ɛse berɛ ne, ɔtra saleɛ bɔ ofi mmokaa mbiri bɔ otimu berɛ daa nu ɔ. Ɔtra nningyein paa bɔ bɛwɔ daa tete mmokaa bɔ bɛwɔ berɛ afebɔɔ nu ɔ; ma sɔ saleɛ ne ɔ́bra Yosef so, ye bɔ baye ye basie ahameɛ bafi oliɛma nemɔ anu.
Benyamin te pataku bɔ ɔkye ngaka di ɔ, ngyerɛmɔ odi naen bɔ ye sa kɔsɔ ye nu ɔ, na nɔsoa ɔkyekyɛ koɛ nu nzesadeɛ.” Yisrael mmusua kure buru ne nyɔ nemɔ ɛne.
Na mmerɛ bɔ né bɛ baba óyira bɛ ne, edwirɛ bɔ ɔha hyirele bɛ hɔ ɛne; ɔfale saleɛ bɔ ɔfata bɛ nu biala yirale ye.
Na ɔhyɛle bɛ kyɛ, “Waha kãa né matoa ne mbanyi mɔ.
Ɔyɛ a ɛ́mɔsie me wɔ me nana mɔ asieleɛ; wɔ nyɔboɛ bɔ wasi sua bɔ yeɛ ɔwɔ Hitiniɛ Efron aseɛ so ne anu.
Mekyire nyɔboɛ bɔ wasi sua bɔ ɔwɔ Makepɛla aseɛ so, wɔ Mamre eyia afiteleɛ, wɔ Kanaan aseɛ so ne.
Ɛhe yeɛ Abraham tɔ fili Hitiniɛ Efron berɛ kyɛ ɔfa yɛ ye asieleɛ ne.
Berɛ yeɛ besiele Abraham ne ɔye Sara; berɛ yeɛ besiele Yisake ne ɔye Rebɛka; na berɛ yeɛ nziele Lea ɔ. Aseɛ ne ɔne nu nyɔboɛ bɔ wasi sua ne, bɛtɔle befili Hitifoɛ sa nu.” Na Yakob hane sɔ dwirɛ ne kitii hyirele ye mma nemɔ yiele ne, ɔpagyale ye gya guale mba ne aso, olele ye nwomeɛ bɔ ɔpɛ ye bo ɔ, na ɔhale nu.
Yosef yakyili ye nwo tole ye baba so, ɔfele ye noa na osuni ye.
Na Yosef hyɛle ye ngoaa safoɛ nemɔ kyɛ bewura ɔse fuin ne ayire amaa wamborɔ.
Yiti bewurale Yisrael fuin ne ayire.
Bɛfale eleburanna yeɛ bɛyɔle ɔ, ofikyɛ né eleburanna yeɛ bɛfa bewura efuin ayire ɔ. Na Misraimfoɛ suni ye eleburasoo.
Na ngyẽa bɔ bɛfa besuni ye ne pɛle nu ne, Yosef sele Faro mbanyi kyɛ, “Sɛ ɛmɔanya baboka me sɔa de a, ye de mesrɛ ɛmɔ, ɛ́mɔfa bɛto Faro nyunu bɛma me kyɛ, me baba maa ndale ndaen na ɔhane kyɛ, ‘Mebaawu, na kosie me wɔ Kanaan aseɛ so, wɔ asieleɛ bɔ mbɛ ndole berɛ kyɛ besie me wɔ nu ne anu.’ Yiti mesrɛ wɔ, maa ngonzie me baba na nza mmra.” Na Faro buale kyɛ, “Kɔ na kosie ɛse, kyɛbɔ ɔmaa ɛtale ndaen ne.” Yiti Yosef hɔle kyɛ ɔkwaasie ɔse; na Faro mbanyi amukoraa: mbanyi bɔ bɛwɔ Faro awuro, yeɛ Misraim maen ne anu mbanyi amukoraa, Yosef awuro ama mukoraa, oliɛma mmienzua mɔ, yeɛ afei ɔse awuro ama mɔ bɛbokale ye so bɛ ne ye hɔle.
Bɛ mma mɔ ne bɛ mmoaen mɔ ne bɛ nandwie mɔ ngome yeɛ bɛhale Gosen aseɛ so ɔ. Teaseɛnam mɔ ne pɔngɔhanɛfoɛ bokale ye so bɛ ne ye hɔle; né ɛlɔen ne te piri paa.
Beedwuli nekaa bɔ bɛboro aburoo wɔ Atade bɔ ɔwɔ asue Yɔɔdan asi dɔ ne, bɛbɔle awuye serɛserɛ bɔ ɔyɛ aworabɔ paa ɔ; na Yosef yɔle ɔse sɛen ɛlɛsoo.
Na Kanaanfoɛ bɔ bɛte aseɛ ne asofoɛ nwuni ɛsɛen bɔ né bɛyɔ wɔ nekaa bɔ bɛboro aburoo wɔ Atade nen, bɛhane kyɛ, “Misraimfoɛ ɛsɛen piri paa ɛhe!” Yiti bɛfrɛle berɛ Abel Misraim.
Ɔwɔ Yɔɔdan asi dɔ.
Yiti Yakob mma mɔ yɔle kyɛbɔ ɔhyɛle bɛ ne ala mane ye; ofikyɛ ye mma nemɔ soale ye hɔle Kanaan aseɛ so, na besiele ye wɔ Makepɛla aseɛ so nyɔboɛ bɔ wasi sua nu wɔ Mamre eyia afiteleɛ.
Abraham tɔle sɔ nyɔboɛ ne ɔne aseɛ ne fili Hitiniɛ Efron berɛ kyɛ ɔfa yɛ ye asieleɛ.
Na Yosef siele ye baba yiele nen, ɔne oliɛma mmienzua nemɔ, yeɛ bɛ bɔ beesomane ye maa osiele ye baba ne amukoraa, besa bɛwale Misraim.
Yosef sá hyɛ oliɛma mɔ bɔ Na Yosef aliɛma nemɔ nwuni kyɛ bɛ baba awu ne, besusuli ye nwo kyɛ, “Anyɔ a, né Yosef atu ye nye wasie yɛ so na watua yɛ bɔne bɔ yayɔ ye ne amu so kerɛ.” Yiti bɛmaa bɛɛhã behyirele Yosef kyɛ, “Wɔ baba hane sɔ dwirɛ ye kitii koraka yeɛ owu ɔ kyɛ, ‘Ɛ́mɔhã behyire Yosef kyɛ, mesrɛ wɔ, fa eliɛma mɔ amumuyɛɛ ne bɛ bɔne kyɛ bɛ, ofikyɛ bɛyɔle wɔ tɛɛ paa.’ Yiti afei, yɛsrɛ wɔ, fa wɔ baba ye Nyameɛ ngoaa mɔ b’amumuyɛɛ kyɛ bɛ.” Na bɛhane ɛhe behyirele Yosef ne, osuni.
Oliɛma nemɔ koso wale beebutubutuli ye nyunu na besele kyɛ, “Yɛte wɔ ngoaa.” Nakoso Yosef sele bɛ kyɛ, “Nnɛma ɛmɔsuro.
Aso ngɔhora ngole Nyameɛ adwuma ngɔyɔ anaa?
Ɛmɔ de, ɛmɔambena me ne paa, nakoso Nyameɛ nhyehyɛleɛ maa ɔkakyili paa; kyɛ ɔnate so okole mmeni pee ngoa, kyɛbɔ afei wala ali ye.
Yiti nnɛma ɛmɔsuro, na ngɔnea ɛmɔ ne ɛmɔ mma mɔ.” Yiti ɔkyekyele bɛ wora mane bɛ kunu tɔle bɛ fɔnwoo.
Yosef wue Yosef ne ɔse awuro ama bɛtenane Misraim, na Yosef lili afoɛ ɛyaa ko ne buru.
Yosef nwuni Efraim ye nana nganzowa mɔ po, na bɛwole Manase awa Makyiri mma bɛtole Yosef gya so.
Yeɛ Yosef sele oliɛma nemɔ kyɛ, “Mebaawu, nakoso Nyameɛ kɔɔnea ɛmɔ.
Na aseɛ bɔ ɔtale ye nwo ndaen hyirele Abraham ne Yisake ne Yakob ne, ɔkɔye ɛmɔ kofi aseɛ he aso ɔkɔfa ɛmɔ kɔhɔ so.” Yosef mane Yisrael mma nemɔ tale ndaen hyirele ye, na ɔhane kyɛ, “Nyameɛ kɔɔye ɛmɔ kofi wa.
Na sɛ ɔba ye sɔ a, ɛ́mɔsoa me mmowue béfi wa bɛhɔ.” Yiti Yosef wuli, mmerɛ bɔ né wali afoɛ ɛyaa ko ne buru ɔ. Bewurale ye ayire bɔ wamma wamborɔ ɔ, na bɛfale ye bɛtole alaka nu wɔ Misraim.
BƆ OLI MOA Dumaa ƐKSADƆSO bo kyire: “AMANDUO.” Amanduo ne te edwirɛ bɔ ohia paa wɔ Yisraelfoɛ abakɔsɛm nu.
Ɔka kyɛbɔ Nyameɛ nate tumi piri so yele ye mmenia Yisraelfoɛ fili Misraim ngoaasolɛ nu.
Besa bɛfrɛ Yisraelfoɛ Hebrifoɛ.
Bahyɛ ƐKSADƆSO nwomaa ne anu nna: Kyɛbɔ Nyameɛ yele Hebrifoɛ fili ngoaasolɛ nu ɔ; Bɔ ɔtole bɛ atunu alaa maa beedwuli Sinai bokaa ne anwo; Nyameɛ ne ye mmenia Hebrifoɛ bɛyɛle apam, apam bɔ okyire bɛ atee bɔ ɔsɛ kyɛ bɛfa so bɛso ye ná bɛbɔ bɛ bra ɔ; Besili ɛtena sua bɔ bɛkɔsɔne Nyameɛ nu ɔ, besiesiele nu, na Nyameɛ mane bɛ ɔsɔfolilɛ ne ɛsɔnenɛ nwo mmeraa.
Nwomaa ne maa yɛnwu nningyein bɔ Nyameɛ yɔle, wɔ mmerɛ bɔ ɔyele ye mmenia fili Misraim ngoaasolɛ nu, ná afei ɔmaa bɛyɛle maen bɔ bele kyẽa bie anyelasoɛ ɔ. Sona bɔ odi dwumaa paa wɔ nwomaa ne anu ole Mose, ofikyɛ ye yeɛ Nyameɛ fale ye tuale ye mmenia noa ɔ. Nwomaa he anu yeɛ Nyameɛ fale Mmeraa Buru ne mane Yisraelfoɛ ɔ .
Nu Dwirɛ Yisraelfoɛ nya fawɔnwodi fi Misraimfoɛ sa nu .—.
a. Bɛyɛ ngoaa wɔ Misraim .- b. Mose aworɛ ne ye ngwadaa nu .—.
d. Mose ne Aarɔn fa bɛ dwirɛ to Misraim hene nyunu .—.
e. Beku Abɔtra boaen; betu befi Misraim .—.
Befi Ɛpo Kɔkorɛ nwo bekoodwu Sinai bokaa ne anwo .—.
Mmeraa ne ne Apam ne .—.
Ɛtena sua ne ɔne ɛsɔnenɛ nwo mmeraa .—.
Bɛhyɛ Yisraelfoɛ anyeborolɛ wɔ Misraim Yisrael mma bɔ bɛ ne Yakob wale Misraim ne, bɛ nu biala ne ye abusua yeɛ ɔwale ɔ. Ye mma nemɔ dumaa ɛhe: Ruben, Simeon, Lewi, Yuda, Yisaka, Sebulɔn, Benyamin, Dan, Nafetali, Gade ne Asɛ.
Né Yakob boso ama ne amukoraa bɛte aburasoo; na né Yosef de ɔwɔ Misraim dada.
Afei Yosef wuli, na oliɛma nemɔ amukoraa ne sɔ aworɛ ndoatoasoɛ ne amukoraa bewuli.
Nakoso Yisrael boso ama nemɔ wowole, bɛ boso trɛle, na bɛ nwo yɛle se.
Yiti beyili maen ne anu tɛkyɛ.
Na ɛhene foforɛ bie bɔ né ɔnze Yosef oolili Misraim bia ne.
Na osele ye mmenia nemɔ kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔnea, Yisraelfoɛ nemɔ asone soma, na b’anwoserɛ bo yɛ so.
Ɛ́mɔma yɛfa bɛ yɛfa nworɛ atee bie aso.
Anyɔ a bɛkɔsone pee, na sɛ koɛ bie ba a, bɛkɔɔboka yɛ pɔfoɛ mɔ ná baho batia yɛ, ná banya atee banwati bafi maen ye anu.” Yiti bɛyeyele adwumayɔlɛfoɛ so mbanyi maa belili bɛ so, kyɛ bɛhyɛ bɛ ma bɛyɔ adwuma bɔ ɔbo bɛ so ɔ. Na bɛkyekyele nguro Pitom ne Ramese maa Faro fa yɛle nekaa bɔ osie ye nningyein ɔ. Nakoso bɛwɔ so bɛ́hyɛ bɛ anyeborolɛ maa ɔbo so nen, bekye po yeɛ né bɛ́kɔ so bɛsone ná bɛtrɛ ɔ. Na Misraimfoɛ surole Yisraelfoɛ paa.
Yiti bɛhyɛle Yisraelfoɛ anyeborolɛ maa bɛyɔle adwuma serɛ paa bɛmane bɛ.
Bɛmane bɛ wora bɔle, ofikyɛ bɛhyɛle bɛ maa bɛyɔle adwuma bɔ ɔbo bɛ so wɔ nnɛterɛ ne mmerekese pɛlɛ nu, fieso adwuma ahoroɔ nu; na bɛhyɛle bɛ anyeborolɛ paa wɔ adwuma biala nu.
Afei Misraim hene sele Hebri mmrasua bɔ bede aworɛ, bɔ bɛ nu ko li Sifra, ná ko wora li Pua ne kyɛ, “Sɛ ɛmɔde Hebri mmrasua aworɛ, ná awoleɛ nu berɛ, ɛmɔnwu kyɛ adɔma ne te bienzua a, odi kyɛ ɛmɔku ye.
Sɛ ɔte brasua de a, nnɛma ɛmɔku ye.” Nakoso né mmrasua bɔ bede aworɛ ne suro Nyameɛ, yiti banyɔ bɔ Misraim hene hyɛle bɛ kyɛ bɛyɔ ne, na mmom bɛmane mmienzua nemɔ nyane bɛ ti didili nu.
Yiti Misraim hene frɛle mmrasua bɔ bede aworɛ ne, na obisale bɛ kyɛ, “Nzu ati yeɛ ɛmɔayɔ sɔ ye, bɔ ɛmɔama mmienzua nemɔ anya bɛ ti badidi nu ye?” Na mmrasua bɔ bede aworɛ ne buale Faro kyɛ, “Hebri mmrasua nemɔ de, bɛtte kyɛ Misraim mmrasua nemɔ; ofikyɛ bɛ nwo te kyerekyerɛɛ, na bɛwo koraka né sona bɔ ode aworɛ ne adwu berɛ.” Yiti Nyameɛ lole mmrasua bɔ bede aworɛ ne, na Yisraelfoɛ nemɔ wora bɛ boso trɛle, na bɛtale pembepembe.
Na ɔnate kyɛ mmrasua bɔ bede aworɛ ne besuro Nyameɛ ne ati, ɔmaa bɛ koso bɛbɔle taen.
Na Faro hyɛle ye mmenia ne amukoraa kyɛ, “Bienzua biala bɔ Hebrifoɛ kɔwo ye ne, ɛ́mɔgyi ye bɛto asue Naele nu, nakoso brasua biala de, ɛ́mɔma onya ngoa.”
Mose aworɛ Biaa bie bɔ ofi Lewi abusua nu oogyale Lewi abusua nu braa.
Braa ne nwonzɛle, na ɔwole baa bienzua.
Na onwuni kyɛ ye nwo yɛ nyemene nen, ɔfale ye feale toonn bosome nza.
Afei de, né ɔfa ye fea a ɔnyɛ yee ko, yiti ɔfale elemmire kɛndɛen, ɔfale pɔweɛ nzue ne ehwaa fale ye nwo, ɔfale adɔma ne tole nu, na ɔɔfale ye siele ngyɛngyɛma nu wɔ asue Naele noa.
Na adɔma n’aliɛma brasua oogyinane dedeede neane bɔ ɔkɔto adɔma ne ɔ. Faro awa brasua wale kyɛ ɔbaabia asue ne anu.
Né ye abaawa nemɔ natenate asue ne noa.
Onwuni kyɛ kɛndɛen ne gyi ngyɛngyɛma ne anu, na ɔsomane ye abaawa ne ko kyɛ ɔɔfa bra.
Obukyele so nen, onwuni adɔma bienzua bɔ osũ ɔ. Ɔyɛle ye anwumvo, na ɔhane kyɛ, “Hebrifoɛ mma ne bie ɛne.” Na adɔma n’aliɛma brasua ne bisale Faro awa brasua ne kyɛ, “Ngɔmvrɛ Hebri mmrasua nemɔ ko mmrɛ wɔ ma ɔma adɔma ne nyɔfone ma wɔ anaa?” Na Faro awa brasua ne buale ye kyɛ, “Yoo, kɔ.” Na abaayaa ne ɔɔfrɛle adɔma ne maame wale.
Na Faro awa brasua ne sele ye kyɛ, “Fa adɔma ne kɔma ye nyɔfone ma me, na ngotua wɔ kerɛ.” Yiti braa ne fale ye hɔle ɔɔmane ye nyɔfone.
Akwadaa ne nyini, na ɔɔfale ye mane Faro awa brasua ne.
Ɔfale ye yɛle ɔwa, na ɔtole ye dumaa Mose, ofikyɛ ɔhane kyɛ, “Nzue nu yeɛ nyele ye mvili ɔ.” Mose nwati kɔ Midian Mose nyini ne, ɛlɛho bie ɔɔpasale oliɛma mɔ Hebrifoɛ nwo, na onwuni adwuma serɛ bɔ né bɛ́hyɛ bɛ maa bɛyɔ ɔ. Na onwuni kyɛ Misraimniɛ bie ɔ́bo oliɛma Hebrifoɛ nemɔ anu ko ɔ. Ɔtotole ye nye bra yiale, na onwuni kyɛ sona biala nne berɛ nen, ohuni Misraimniɛ ne, na ɔfale ye feale anweaa nu.
Aleɛ hyene ne, ofitele, edwirɛ nwanwa, onwuni Hebrifoɛ nyɔ kyɛ bɛ́ko ɔ. Na obisale bɔ ye dwirɛ nyɛ fɛ ne kyɛ, “Nzu ati yeɛ ɛ́bo eliɛngo ɔ?” Na obuale kyɛ, “Nwa yeɛ ɔyɛle wɔ yɛ so panyi ne ndɛenbualɛniɛ ɔ?
Ɛpena kyɛ eku me kyɛbɔ ehuni Misraimniɛ ne anaa?” Yiti edwirɛ ne mane Mose surole, na ɔhane ye ye ti anu kyɛ, “Eh, edwirɛ ne afite amba!” Na Faro tele sɔ dwirɛ nen, ɔyɛle kyɛ okohu Mose.
Nakoso Mose nwatili Faro, na ɔɔtenane Midian maen nu wɔ abura bie anwo.
Né Midian sɔfo le mmaa mmrasua nzoo, na bɛwale berɛ kyɛ bɛbaato nzue begua nningyein bɔ bɛ baba nyɛmmoa no nu nzue ne anu.
Mmoaenneafoɛ biemɔ wale bɛɛfoane bɛ, nakoso Mose dwɔsole, ohuru gyinane bɛ si, na ɔmane mmoaen nemɔ nzue.
Na besa bɛwale bɛ baba Rewel berɛ nen, obisale bɛ kyɛ, “Nzu ati yeɛ ɛnɛ de ɛmɔawa ndɛ sɔa ye?” Bebuale kyɛ, “Misraimniɛ bie lele yɛ fili mmoaenneafoɛ nemɔ sa nu, ɔtole nzue mane yɛ po, na ɔmane yɛ mmoaen nemɔ nzue.” Na obisale ye mma mmrasua nemɔ kyɛ, “Ɔwɔ nisua?
Nzu ati yeɛ ɛmɔayakyi biaa ne dɔ ɔ?
Ɛmɔɔfrɛ ye ma oodidi.” Mose penene so ɔne biaa ne bɛtenane, na ɔfale ɔwa brasua Sipora mane Mose gyale.
Sipora wole baa bienzua, na Mose tole ye dumaa Gɛsɔm, ɔnate kyɛ Mose hane kyɛ, “Maayɛ ɛwɔfoɛ wɔ amanvrafoɛ aseɛ so.” Afoɛ pee pɛle nu, na Misraim hene wuli.
Afei Yisraelfoɛ nwuni ngoaasolɛ nu amaneɛ piri paa; bɛbɔle awuye, na bɛ suɛ wɔ ngoaasolɛ nu ne dwuli Nyameɛ nyunu.
Nyameɛ tele b’awuyebɔlɛ ne, na ɔkayele apam bɔ ɔne Abraham, Yisake ne Yakob bɛyɛle ne.
Nyameɛ neane Yisraelfoɛ nemɔ, na bɛyɛle ye anwumvo.
Nyameɛ frɛ Mose Né Mose yeɛ ɔnea ye sia Yɛtro, bɔ ɔte Midian sɔfo ne mmoaen so ɔ. Ɛlɛho bie, ɔhane mmoaen ne hɔle dedeede wɔ ɛserɛ ne noa dɔ paa, na oodwuli Nyameɛ bokaa Horebo nye abo.
Na AWURADE abɔfo yele ye nwo ali hyirele ye wɔ ngyɛkyerɛ bie bɔ né ogye wuronyiwuronyi nu.
Mose neane, edwirɛ nwanwa, onwuni kyɛ ngyɛkyerɛ ne ogye de, nakoso né ɔnyera.
Na Mose hane kyɛ, “Edwirɛ nwanwa he de, mémakye mékɔ dɔ mekɔnea nikyee ti bɔ ɔmma ngyɛkyerɛ ne nyera ne.” Na AWURADE nwuni kyɛ wamakye wafa dɔ ɔkwaanea nen, ɔfrɛle ye fili ngyɛkyerɛ ne anu kyɛ, “Mose!
Mose!
Na osurole kyɛ, “Me ɛhe.” Na AWURADE hane kyɛ, “Nnɛpingye wa!
Puropuro wɔ gya nu mbaboa ne, ofikyɛ nekaa bɔ egyi ne te aseɛ krongron.” Na ɔfa sɔle so kyɛ, “Me ole wɔ baba Nyameɛ ne, Abraham Nyameɛ ne, Yisake Nyameɛ ne Yakob Nyameɛ ne.
Na Mose fale ye nyunu feale, ofikyɛ né osuro kyɛ ɔkɔnea Nyameɛ ɔ. Na AWURADE hane kyɛ, “Me mmenia bɔ bɛwɔ Misraim ne, manwu b’amaneɛnwunɛ ne, na mate awuye bɔ b’adwuma so mbanyi mɔ maa bɛbɔ ne.
Manwu b’amaneɛnwunɛ ne.
Na madwu mawa ase kyɛ mebaale bɛ mefi Misraimfoɛ sa nu, ná meye bɛ mefi sɔ aseɛ ne aso mekɔ aseɛ paa bɔ ɔtrɛ ɔ so, aseɛ bɔ nyɔfonesue ne woɛ tengyɛ wɔ so ne: Kanaanfoɛ, Hitifoɛ, Amorifoɛ, Perisifoɛ, Hiwifoɛ ne Yebusifoɛ maen ne.
Afei de, awuye bɔ Yisraelfoɛ bɛbɔ ne wadwu me nyunu, na manwu ɛhyɛlɛ bɔ Misraimfoɛ bɛhyɛ bɛ ne.
Yiti bra.
Mésoma wɔ maa ɛkɔ Faro berɛ ɛkɔye me mmenia Yisraelfoɛ efi Misraim!” Nakoso Mose bisale Nyameɛ kyɛ, “Me ole nwa bɔ mékɔ Faro berɛ mekɔye Yisraelfoɛ mefi Misraim ɔ?” Na Nyameɛ sele ye kyɛ, “Ngoli wɔ si.
Na bɔ okohyire kyɛ me yeɛ mésoma wɔ ɛhe: sɛ ɛye maen ne fi Misraim ba a, sɔ bokaa he aso yeɛ ɛmɔkɔsɔne Nyameɛ ɔ.” Na Mose bisale Nyameɛ kyɛ, “Sɛ mekɔ Yisraelfoɛ berɛ, ná mekã mekyire bɛ kyɛ, ‘Ɛmɔ nana mɔ Nyameɛ yeɛ wasoma me ɔ,’ ná bɛ wora bebisa me kyɛ, ‘Ye dumaa li sɛɛ’ a, nzikyɛ dwirɛ yeɛ nga ngyire bɛ ɔ?” Na Nyameɛ buale Mose kyɛ, “ME ALA OLE ME ALA.” Na osele kyɛ, “Bɔ ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛkã kyire Yisraelfoɛ hɔ ɛhe: ‘ME ALA asoma me ɛmɔ berɛ.’ ” Nyameɛ sa sele Mose kyɛ, “Kã kyire Yisraelfoɛ kyɛ, ‘AWURADE ɛmɔ nana mɔ Nyameɛ ne, Abraham Nyameɛ ne, Yisake Nyameɛ ne, Yakob Nyameɛ ne yeɛ wasoma me ɛmɔ berɛ ɔ.’ Me dumaa bɔ ɔwɔ berɛ afebɔɔ hɔ ɛne, na ɛhe yeɛ aworɛ ndoatoasoɛ mukoraa bɛkɔfa bɛkɔfrɛ me ɔ. Kɔ!
Kɔboaboa Yisrael mbanyi mɔ noa, ná kã kyire bɛ kyɛ, ‘AWURADE ɛmɔ nana mɔ Nyameɛ ne, Abraham Nyameɛ ne, Yisake Nyameɛ ne, Yakob Nyameɛ ne, waye ye nwo ali wahyire me.
Ɔnwa: ‘Maanea ɛmɔ, na manwu nikyee bɔ bɛfa bɛyɔ ɛmɔ wɔ Misraim ne.
Na mayɛ m’adwene kyɛ ngɔye ɛmɔ ngofi Misraim amaneɛnwunɛ nu, ná mafa ɛmɔ mahɔ Kanaanfoɛ, Hitifoɛ, Amorifoɛ, Perisifoɛ, Hiwifoɛ ne Yebusifoɛ aseɛ ne aso, aseɛ bɔ nyɔfonesue ne woɛ tengyɛ wɔ so ne.
“Bekotie wɔ dwirɛ, na ɛne Yisrael mbanyi bɛhɔ Misraim hene berɛ beese ye kyɛ, ‘AWURADE, Hebrifoɛ Nyameɛ ne, ɔne yɛ ayia.
Yiti yɛsrɛ wɔ, ma yɛ ate ma yɛhɔ atee bɔ bɛfa ɛlɛsa bɛpɛ ɔ wɔ ɛserɛ so, ná yɛɛbɔ afɔleɛ yɛma AWURADE yɛ Nyameɛ ne.’ Me de, mese kyɛ Misraim hene ngɔma ɛmɔ ate ma ɛmɔngɔhɔ, sana tumi piri bie hyɛ ye so koraka.
Yiti ngɔtengyɛ me sa ngɔfa anwanwadeɛ mukoraati bɔ ngɔyɔ ye Misraim ne ngotia Misraim, na ɛhe asi ne, ɔkɔma ɛmɔ kɔhɔ.
Ngɔma Misraimfoɛ kɔlo mmenia hemɔ, amaa sɛ ɛ́mɔfi berɛ a, ɛmɔangɔ ye nzanza.
Yisrael brasua biala kobisa ɛdwetɛ ne sikaa kɔkorɛ mbembenanneɛ ne ndena kofi Misraim brasua bɔ ɔne ye bɛte bepingye ɔ berɛ, ɔne Misraim brasua biala bɔ ɔte ye awuro ɔ berɛ, na ɛmɔkɔfa sɔ nningyein ne bekosiesie ɛmɔ mma mmienzua ne mmrasua mɔ nwo.
Na ɛhe kɔmaa ɛmɔkonya koɛ nu nzesadeɛ bekofi Misraimfoɛ berɛ.”
Nyameɛ ma Mose tumi nwanwasoɛ Na Mose buale kyɛ, “Sɛ banne me banni, anaakyɛ bandie me dwirɛ, ná bɛka kyɛ, ‘AWURADE anye ye nwo ali wangyire wɔ huu’ ɛ?’ ” Na AWURADE bisale ye kyɛ, “Nzikyɛ yeɛ otira wɔ sa nu ye?” Obuale kyɛ, “Pɔmaa ɔ.” Na AWURADE sele kyɛ, “Gyi to aseɛnwo berɛ!” Ogyi tole berɛ, na ɔkakyili ewoo.
Na Mose pimbini ye si fili ye nwo.
Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Tengyɛ wɔ sa sɔ ye dua ne anu.” Ɔtengyɛle ye sa sɔle ye nu, na ɔkakyili pɔmaa wɔ ye sa nu.
Na AWURADE sele kyɛ, “Ɛhe kɔmaa bekole bekoli kyɛ AWURADE, bɛ nana mɔ Nyameɛ ne, Abraham Nyameɛ ne, Yisake Nyameɛ ne, Yakob Nyameɛ ne yeɛ waye ye nwo ali wahyire wɔ ɔ.” Na AWURADE sá sele ye kyɛ, “Fa wɔ sa wura wɔ hue so.” Ɔfale ye sa wurale ye hue so, na ɔyele ye sa fili ye hue so nen, né kwata ayɛ ye sa ne amaa wayɛ fufue kyɛ asukɔtwea.
Na AWURADE sele ye kyɛ, “Fa wɔ sa wura wɔ hue so bieku.” Ɔfale ye sa wurale ye hue so bieku, na ɔyele ye sa ne fitele nen, né wasa wakakyi kyɛ ye nwonaen ngaa ne ala. Na Nyameɛ sele kyɛ, “Sɛ banne wɔ banni, anaakyɛ banne sɛngyerɛnneɛ bɔ oli moa ne bando nu a, bekole bɔ ɔtɔ so nyɔ ne bekoli.
Na sɛ banne sɔ nzɛngyerɛnneɛ nyɔ ne po banni, anaa bandie wɔ dwirɛ a, ye de sa asue Naele nzue ne bie, ná hwie gua aseɛ wosee so.
Na Naele nu nzue bɔ ɛkɔsa ne kɔkakyi mogya wɔ aseɛ wosee ne aso.” Na Mose sele AWURADE kyɛ, “Mesrɛ wɔ, AWURADE.
Ofi me tetetete bɔ ɔbaadwu ɛnɛ bɔ ɛne w’akoaa bedwudwo ye, nnde sona bɔ ye noa ate ɔ; me dwudwolɛ te nyaanyaa, na me temverema abutu.” Na AWURADE bisale ye kyɛ, “Nwa yeɛ ɔyɔle kuro sona noa ɔ?
Nwa yeɛ ɔmaa ɔyɛ emumu anaa asotiniwaaniɛ, ɔmaa onwu nikye anaa ɔyɛ ye anyesiniwaaniɛ ɔ?
Yiti nna me AWURADE ɔ?
Yiti kɔ, na ngɔma wɔ noa kɔte ná mahyire wɔ bɔ ɛha ɔ.” Nakoso Mose sele kyɛ, “Yieee!
AWURADE, mesrɛ wɔ ala, soma sona foforɛ.” Afei AWURADE fɛle Mose so yaa maa ɔhane kyɛ, “Eliɛma Aarɔn, bɔ ɔte Lewiniɛ ne, ɔnne berɛ hɔ ɔ?
Mese kyɛ ye noa ate.
Tie, wasi nu ɔbaayia wɔ, na sɛ onwu wɔ a, ɔkɔyɛ ye fɛ soma.
Ka edwirɛ ne kyire ye, ná fa edwirɛ ne tua ye noa; na ngɔmaa ɛne ye ɛmɔ noa kodwu dwaa nu, ná mahyire ɛmɔ bɔ ɛmɔhã ɔ. Okogyina wɔ gya nu kodwudwo kohyire mmenia ne, wɔ noa dwirɛ kotua ye noa, ná wɔ wora ayɛ kyɛ Nyameɛ ama ye.
Fa pɔmaa he tira, na ye yeɛ ɛkɔfa kɔyɔ nzɛngyerɛnneɛ ɔ.” Mose sá kɔ Misraim Mose sá hɔle ye sia Yɛtro berɛ, na osele ye kyɛ; “Mesrɛ wɔ, maa nza ngɔ nniɛma mɔ berɛ wɔ Misraim, ná ngɔnea sɛ bɛtɛ te ase a.” Na Yɛtro sele Mose kyɛ, “Kɔ asomdwee nu oo.” Na AWURADE sele Mose wɔ Midian kyɛ, “Sá kɔ Misraim, ofikyɛ bɛ bɔ né bɛpena wɔ beku wɔ ne, bɛ mukoraa bawu.” Yiti Mose fale ɔye ne ye mma mmienzua nyɔ ne tenatenane afunum so, na osa hɔle Misraim aseɛ so.
Na ɔfale Nyameɛ pɔmaa ne tirale.
Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Sɛ esa kɔ Misraim a, nea kyɛ anwanwadeɛ mukoraa bɔ mama wɔ tumi kyɛ ɛyɔ ne, ɛkɔyɔ ye Faro nyunu.
Nakoso ngɔma ye so kɔyɛ se, bɔ ɔnate so ɔngɔma me mmenia nemɔ ngɔhɔ ɔ. Afei ka kyire Faro kyɛ, ‘AWURADE nwa: Yisrael te me bamuɛbaa bienzua.
Na mekã mekyire wɔ kyɛ, “Ma mma ne ɔhɔ ɔɔsɔne me.” Na sɛ amma ye ate ma wangɔ a, ngohũ wɔ bamuɛbaa bienzua.’ ” Na Mose sili nu ne, AWURADE yiale ye wɔ asikyeleɛ bie anu wɔ atunu, na ɔyɛle kyɛ okohu Mose.
Nakoso Sipora fale twerɛboɛ bie pɛle ɔwa ne bienzua, ɔfa hane Mose gya, na ɔhane kyɛ, “Amba, ɔnate sɔ amaneɛ he aso, aayɛ me bɔbɔ deinn me busuaniɛ!” Yiti AWURADE yakyili ye.
Na ɔnate bienzuapɛlɛ ne ati, Sipora sele kyɛ, “Ɛte mogya nu atɔmvorɛ biaa.” AWURADE sele Aarɔn kyɛ, “Kɔ ɛserɛ so dɔ koyia Mose.” Yiti ɔhɔle, oyiale ye wɔ Nyameɛ bokaa ne anwo, na ɔfele ye noa.
Mose fale AWURADE dwirɛ bɔ wafa wasoma ye ne amukoraa, ɔne nzɛngyerɛnneɛ bɔ wahyɛ ye kyɛ ɔyɔ ne nwo amaneɛ bɔle Aarɔn.
Afei Mose ne Aarɔn hɔle bɛɛboaboale Yisrael mbanyi mukoraa noa.
Aarɔn fale edwirɛ amukoraa bɔ Nyameɛ aha ahyire Mose ne tole dwaa, na ɔyɔle nzɛngyerɛnneɛ ne wɔ mmenia ne nyunu berɛ.
Mmenia ne le lili.
Na bɛtele kyɛ AWURADE aapasa Yisraelfoɛ nwo, ná wanwu b’amaneɛnwunɛ nen, bɛbɔle bɛ ti ase bɛsɔnene ye.
Mose ne Aarɔn gyi Faro nyunu Nziɛ ye, Mose ne Aarɔn hɔle Faro berɛ beesele ye kyɛ, “AWURADE Yisrael Nyameɛ nwa: ‘Ma me mmenia nemɔ bɛhɔ, ná beeli aluolue bɛma me wɔ ɛserɛ so.’ ” Nakoso Faro buale kyɛ, “AWURADE ne ole nwa bɔ ɔsɛ kyɛ metie ye ná mema Yisraelfoɛ bɛkɔ ɔ?
Menze sɔ AWURADE ne, yeɛ Yisraelfoɛ koso mengɔma bɛngɔhɔ!” Na besele kyɛ, “Hebrifoɛ Nyameɛ ne ɔne yɛ ayia, yiti yɛsrɛ wɔ, ma yɛ ate ma yɛhɔ atee bɔ bɛfa ɛlɛsa bɛpɛ ɔ wɔ ɛserɛ so, ná yɛɛbɔ afɔleɛ yɛma AWURADE yɛ Nyameɛ ne; na anyɔ a né wafa ewue anwonyerɛ anaa ngrandɛ wawa yɛ so.” Nakoso Misraim hene sele bɛ kyɛ, “Mose ne Aarɔn, nzu ati yeɛ ɛmɔpena kyɛ bɛma mmenia ne yakyi b’adwuma bɔ bɛyɔ ne ɔ?
Ɛmɔhɔ bɛɛtoa ɛmɔ adwuma serɛ ne aso!” Na Faro sá sele kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔtie, afei bɔ maen ne anu mmenia asone pee ne yeɛ ɛmɔmaa bɛyakyi adwumayɔlɛ ɔ!” Sɔ kyẽa ne ala, Faro hyɛle maen adwumayɔlɛfoɛ mɔ so mbanyi, yeɛ adwumayɔlɛfoɛ mɔ so neafoɛ mɔ kyɛ, “Nnɛmɔma mmenia nemɔ ɛserɛ ko maa bɛpɛ mmerekese kyɛbɔ daa ne ɛmɔyɔle ne, na mmom ɛ́mɔma bɛ bɔbɔ bɛɛpena ɛserɛ ne.
Mmerekese somaa bɔ né bɛpɛ ye daa ne, ɛ́mɔma bɛ́pɛ sɔ ala. Nnɛma ɛmɔte so, ofikyɛ bɛte foen, na ɛhe ati yeɛ ɔmaa besu kyɛ, ‘Maa yɛhɔ yɛɛbɔ afɔleɛ yɛma yɛ Nyameɛ ne.’ Ɛ́mɔma mmenia nemɔ adwuma bɔ ɔyɛ se paa ma bɛyɔ, amaa bandie nnakannaka dwirɛ biala.
Yiti maen adwumayɔlɛfoɛ mɔ so mbanyi, yeɛ adwumayɔlɛfoɛ mɔ so neafoɛ mɔ hɔle beesele mmenia ne kyɛ, “Faro nwa: ‘Mengɔma ɛmɔ ɛserɛ ko.’ Ɛmɔ bɔbɔ bɛɛpena ɛserɛ wɔ nekaa biala bɔ ɛmɔkonya bie ɔ; nakoso ɛmɔ adwuma ne de, yɛngɔte so kaala.
Yiti mmenia ne tele bɛ nwo guale Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa bɛɛboaboale atokoɔ mmakaa wuruwaa noa bɛfa bɛkakyili ɛserɛ.
Adwumayɔlɛfoɛ so mbanyi nemɔ hane bɛ bo kyɛ, “Odi kyɛ ɛmɔyie ɛmɔ daa daa adwuma ne, kyɛbɔ ɛserɛ wɔ berɛ ne ɛmɔyɔle ne ala!” Bɛbole Yisrael mbanyi bɔ Faro adwumayɔlɛfoɛ mɔ so mbanyi afa adwuma ne awura bɛ sa ne, na bebisale bɛ kyɛ, “Mmerekese somaa bɔ ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛmɔpɛ ye anoma ne ɛnɛ ne, nzu ati yeɛ ɛmɔambɛ ye mu, kyɛbɔ dáa ɛmɔpɛ ne?” Afei Yisrael mbanyi bɔ bafa adwuma ne bawura bɛ sa ne wale Faro berɛ beesuni behyirele ye kyɛ, “Nzu ati yeɛ ɛfa sɔ dwirɛ he di wɔ ngoaa ɔ?
Bɛmma wɔ ngoaa ɛserɛ biala, nakoso bese yɛ kyɛ, ‘Ɛ́mɔpɛ mmerekese!’ Bɛbo wɔ ngoaa, nakoso mvomsoɛ ne fi wɔ mmenia ne.” Na Faro buale kyɛ, “Ɛmɔte foen, ɛmɔte foen soma!
Sɔ ati yeɛ ɛmɔnwa: ‘Ma yɛ ate ma yɛɛbɔ afɔleɛ yɛma AWURADE’ ne.
Ɛmɔhã bɛ nwo bɛɛyɔ adwuma!
Bɛngɔma ɛmɔ ɛserɛ biala, nakoso mmerekese somaa bɔ ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛmɔpɛ ne ala yeɛ ɛmɔkɔpɛ ɔ.” Yisrael mbanyi bɔ adwuma ne wura bɛ sa nwuni kyɛ edwirɛ ato bɛ, wɔ mmerɛ bɔ bɛha behyirele bɛ kyɛ, “Mmerekese somaa bɔ ɛlɛho biala ɛmɔpɛ ne, ɛmɔngɔte so.” Befili Faro berɛ bɛ́ba nen, bɛɛtole Mose ne Aarɔn kyɛ bɛnwondɛ bɛ.
Na besele bɛ kyɛ, “Nyameɛ ɔ́nea ɛmɔ na óbua ɛmɔ ndɛen, ofikyɛ ɛmɔamaa yayɛ tɛɛ wɔ Faro ne ye mbanyi nyunu, na ɛmɔafa ngrandɛ bawura bɛ sa nu kyɛ behũ yɛ.” Mose bɔ Nyameɛ somoɛ Afei Mose sá sele AWURADE kyɛ, “Oo AWURADE, nzu ati yeɛ ama edwirɛ sɔaa ato mmenia ye mɔ ɔ?
Nzu ati yeɛ ɛsomane me ɔ?
Ofi mmerɛ bɔ mmale Faro berɛ, ná ndwudwole wɔ dumaa nu ɔ, ɛhalɛ alaa yeɛ ɔha mmenia ye mɔ ɔ, nakoso ɛyyɔle wɔ mmenia ye mɔ bɛ lelɛ nwo hwee.”
Na AWURADE buale Mose kyɛ, “Afei de, ɛbaanwu nikyee bɔ ngɔfa ngɔyɔ Faro ɔ. Ofikyɛ, tumi piri kɔha ye kɔme asi maa ɔkɔyakyi bɛ maa bɛkɔhɔ; tumi piri kɔha ye kɔme asi maa ɔkɔfoa bɛ kofi ye aseɛ so.” Mose frɛlɛ nwo dwirɛ bieku Nyameɛ sele Mose kyɛ, “Me ole AWURADE.
Nyele me nwo ali ngyirele Abraham, Yisake ne Yakob kyɛ nde Tuminiɛ Nyameɛ.
Nakoso me dumaa YAHWE (AWURADE) ne de, mamma bangyina so bannwu me.
Mene bɛ koso yɛyɛle m’apam, kyɛ ngɔfa Kanaan aseɛ bɔ bɛɛtenane so bɛyɛle ɛwɔfoɛ ne ngɔma bɛ.
Asa koso, Yisraelfoɛ bɔ Misraimfoɛ afa bɛ ayɛ nganga ne, mate awuye bɔ bɛbɔ ne, na makaye m’apam ne.
Yiti ka kyire Yisraelfoɛ kyɛ, “Me ole AWURADE, na ngɔye ɛmɔ ngofi Misraim amaneɛnwunɛ nu, ná male ɛmɔ mafi bɛ ngoaasolɛ nu.
Na ɔnate tumi asaa ne asohwenɛ mbiri mbiri so yeɛ ngɔfa ngole ɛmɔ ɔ. Ngɔfa ɛmɔ ngɔyɛ me mmenia, ná me wora ngɔyɛ ɛmɔ Nyameɛ.
Na ɛmɔkonwu ye kyɛ me ole AWURADE ɛmɔ Nyameɛ bɔ olele ɛmɔ fili Misraim amaneɛnwunɛ nu ne.
Aseɛ bɔ mata ndaen kyɛ ngɔfa ngɔma Abraham, Yisake ne Yakob nen, ngɔfa ɛmɔ ngɔhɔ so.
Ngɔfa ngɔma ɛmɔ maa ɔkɔyɛ ɛmɔ deɛ.
Me ole AWURADE.’ ” Mose hane sɔ dwirɛ ne hyirele Yisraelfoɛ nemɔ, nakoso ɔnate b’aba nu bɔ né wabu, ɔne ngoaasolɛ serɛserɛ bɔ né bɛwɔ nu ne ati, bandɛ ye so.
Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Kɔ, kɔha kyire Misraim hene Faro kyɛ ɔyakyi Yisraelfoɛ mɔ ma befi ye aseɛ so bɛhɔ.” Nakoso Mose buale AWURADE kyɛ, “Yisraelfoɛ po bandie me, ɔkɔyɛ sɛɛ né Faro atie me, me bɔ me noa ɔttele ɔ?” AWURADE ne Mose ne Aarɔn dwudwole, na ɔhyɛle bɛ kyɛ bɛɛhã sɔ dwirɛ ne behyire Yisraelfoɛ, ɔne Misraim hene Faro, ná bɛ́ye Yisraelfoɛ béfi Misraim aseɛ so.
Mbanyi bɔ né bɛlela b’abusua nemɔ noa ɛhe: Yisrael bamuɛbaa Ruben ye mma mɔ: Hanoke, Palu, Hesron ne Karemi.
Ruben abusua mɔ ɛne.
Simeon mma mɔ: Yemuel, Yamin, Ohade, Yakin, Soha, yeɛ Sɔɔlo bɔ oni te Kanaanniɛ ne.
Simeon abusua mɔ ɛne.
Lewi mma mɔ dumaa, kyɛbɔ b’aworɛ ndoatoasoɛ si te hɔ ɛhe: Gɛsɔn, Kohate ne Merari.
Lewi afoɛ bɔ olili te ɛyaa ko aburasa ne nzoo.
Gɛsɔn mma mɔ ɛhe: Libini ne Simei, bɛ ne b’abusua mɔ.
Kohate mma mɔ ɛhe: Amram, Yisare, Hebron ne Yusiɛl.
Kohate afoɛ bɔ olili te ɛyaa ko ne aburasa ne nza.
Merari mma mɔ ɛhe: Maheli ne Musi.
Lewi abusua nemɔ, kyɛbɔ b’aworɛ ndoatoasoɛ te ɛne.
Amram gyale ye baba aliɛma brasua Yokebɛde, na ɔne ye bɛwole Aarɔn ne Mose.
Amram afoɛ bɔ olili te ɛyaa ko ne aburasa ne nzoo.
Yisare mma mɔ ɛhe: Kora, Nefege ne Sikri.
Yusiɛl mma mɔ ɛhe: Misael, Elsafan ne Sitri.
Aarɔn gyale Aminadabo awa brasua Elihyeba bɔ oliɛma ole Nason ne.
Na ɔne ye bɛwole Nadabo, Abihu, Eleasa ne Yitama.
Kora mma mɔ ɛhe: Asire, Ɛlkana ne Abiasafe.
Kora abusua mɔ ɛne.
Aarɔn awa Eleasa gyale Putiel mma mmrasua nemɔ ko, na ɔne ye bɛwole Finehase.
Lewi abusua kure ne, nu abusua mbanyi bɔ bɛlela ye noa ɛne.
Aarɔn ne Mose ole mmenia bɔ AWURADE ha hyirele bɛ kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔye Yisraelfoɛ béfi Misraim aseɛ so, kyɛbɔ bɛ kure kure si te ɔ.” Mose ne Aarɔn komapɛ ne ala yeɛ bɛfa bɛtole Misraim hene Faro nyunu kyɛ ɔ́ma Yisraelfoɛ bétu béfi Misraim ɔ. Nyameɛ sá hyɛ Mose bɔ Kyẽa bɔ AWURADE ne Mose dwudwole wɔ Misraim aseɛ so ne, AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Me ole AWURADE.
Kã edwirɛ bɔ mekã mekyire wɔ ne amukoraa kyire Misraim hene Faro.” Nakoso Mose buale AWURADE wɔ ye nyunu berɛ kyɛ, “Yieee!
Me noa ɔttele, ɔkɔyɛ sɛɛ né Faro atie me dwirɛ?”
Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Tie, mayɛ wɔ kyɛ Nyameɛ wɔ Faro nye so, na eliɛma Aarɔn kɔyɛ wɔ ngɔmhyɛlɛniɛ.
Ka bɔ mahyɛ wɔ kyɛ ɛha ne amukoraati; na eliɛma Aarɔn kɔha kohyire Faro kyɛ ɔyakyi Yisraelfoɛ ate ma befi ye aseɛ so bɛhɔ.
Nakoso ngɔma Faro kɔyɛ asobrakyeɛ.
Ɔwɔ nu kyɛ ngɔma me nzɛngyerɛnneɛ ne anwanwadeɛ kɔsone pee wɔ Misraim aseɛ so de, nakoso Faro ngɔtɛ ɛmɔ so.
Ngɔfa me tumi ngɔhwe Misraim so, na ngɔfa asohwenɛ piri so ngɔye me lɔen, me mmenia Yisraelfoɛ, ngofi Misraim aseɛ so.
Na sɛ metengyɛ me sa wɔ Misraim so, ná meye Yisraelfoɛ mefi bɛ nu a, Misraimfoɛ konwu kyɛ me ole AWURADE.” Na kyɛbɔ AWURADE hyɛle Mose ne Aarɔn kyɛ bɛyɔ ne, sɔ ala yeɛ bɛyɔle ɔ. Mmerɛ bɔ bɛ ne Faro dwudwole nen, né Mose ali afoɛ aburawɔtwɛ, yeɛ Aarɔn koso afoɛ aburawɔtwɛ ne nza.
Aarɔn pɔmaa ne Na AWURADE sele Mose ne Aarɔn kyɛ, “Sɛ Faro ka kyire ɛmɔ kyɛ, ‘Ɛ́mɔyɔ sɛngyerɛnneɛ bie behyire a, ye de ka kyire Aarɔn kyɛ, ‘Gyi wɔ pɔmaa ne to Faro nyunu berɛ ma ɔkakyi ewoo.’ ” Yiti Mose ne Aarɔn hɔle Faro berɛ bɛɛyɔle kyɛbɔ AWURADE hyɛle bɛ ne.
Aarɔn gyili ye pɔmaa ne tole Faro ne ye mbanyi mɔ nyunu berɛ, na ɔkakyili ewoo.
Faro koso frɛfrɛle mmenia bɔ bɛse ase, ɔne musueyelɛfoɛ maa bɛwale, na sɔ Misraim ngonyaayelɛfoɛ nemɔ koso yele ngonyaa yɔle sɔ ala. Bɛ mukoraa begyili bɛ mbɔmaa nemɔ beguale aseɛnwo berɛ, na bɛkakyilikakyili ewoo mɔ.
Nakoso Aarɔn pɔmaa ne memene bɛ mbɔmaa nemɔ.
Bekye po yeɛ Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so ɔ, na wandɛ bɛ so, kyɛbɔ AWURADE hane ne ala. Nzue kakyi mogya Afei AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Faro abubu mmakaa watua ye so, na ɔngɔpene ma mmenia ne ngɔhɔ.
Kɔ Faro berɛ ngyerɛmɔ, mmerɛ bɔ ófite kɔ asue Naele noa ɔ. Kogyina asue ne noa berɛ nwondɛ ye, ná fa wɔ pɔmaa bɔ ɔkakyili ewoo ne tira.
Na ka kyire ye kyɛ, AWURADE, Hebrifoɛ Nyameɛ ne asoma me kyɛ mmanga ngyire wɔ kyɛ, ‘Ma me mmenia nemɔ bɛhɔ bɛɛsɔne me wɔ ɛserɛ so, nakoso abubu mmakaa atua wɔ so maa waadwu bekye.’ AWURADE nwa nyoo, ‘Bɔ ɔkɔmaa ekonwu ye kyɛ nde AWURADE ɛhe: Tie, ngɔfa pɔmaa bɔ otira me sa nu ne ngofĩ asue Naele nu, na nzue ne kɔkakyi mogya.
Naen bɔ bɛwɔ asue Naele nu kowuwu, nzue ne kɔbo mvamva, na Misraimfoɛ ngɔhora ngɔno Naele nzue.’ ” Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Ka kyire Aarɔn kyɛ, ‘Fa wɔ pɔmaa ne, ná tengyɛ wɔ sa wɔ Misraim nzue mɔ so: b’asue mbiri mɔ, Naele sa mɔ, b’abura mɔ ne b’ɛkwaa mukoraa so ma bɛkakyi mogya.
Misraim aseɛ ne aso mukoraa kɔyɛ mogya, bua ne angora mɔ anu po.’ ” Mose ne Aarɔn yɔle kyɛbɔ AWURADE hyɛle bɛ ne ala. Aarɔn mane ye pɔmaa ne aso hɔle anwuro wɔ Faro ne ye mbanyi mɔ nyunu berɛ, ɔfa fini asue Naele nu, na Naele nzue amukoraa kakyili mogya.
Nzue ne anu naen wuwuli, na Naele nzue bone mvamvamvamva bɔ Misraimfoɛ angora bie no ɔ. Na Misraim aseɛ ne aso amukoraa yɛle mogya.
Nakoso Misraim ngonyaayelɛfoɛ koso yele ngonyaa yɔle sɔ ala. Yiti Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, na wandɛ bɛ so, kyɛbɔ AWURADE hane ne ala. Faro sá hɔle ye awuro, na wamva ɛhe po wanyɛ dwirɛ.
Na Misraimfoɛ amukoraa tutuli abura wɔ asue Naele noa bɛpenane nzue bɔ bɛkɔno ɔ, ofikyɛ bangora Naele nzue no.
AWURADE sɛkyele asue Naele nen, ngyẽa ɛlɛsoo pɛle nu.
Mborohyɛen manyamanya Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Kɔ Faro berɛ kose ye kyɛ, ‘AWURADE nwa nyoo: Ma me mmenia nemɔ ate ma bɛhɔ, ná bɛɛsɔne me.
Nakoso sɛ amma bɛ ate ma bangɔ a, ngɔma mborohyɛen kɔto kɔpete maen ne anu amukoraa.
Mborohyɛen koyi asue Naele nu to, bekofi nu bɛkɔwa w’awuro, bɛkɔwa wɔ sua nu ne wɔ bɛen so, wɔ mbanyi mɔ ne wɔ mmenia awuro, wɔ bokyea mɔ ne wɔ ngukue mɔ nu.
Na mborohyɛen nemɔ kɔwa wɔ so, wɔ mmenia ne wɔ mbanyi mukoraa so.’ ” Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Ka kyire Aarɔn kyɛ, ‘Tengyɛ wɔ sa, ná fa wɔ pɔmaa ne kyire asue mbiri mɔ so, asue Naele sa mɔ so, ɔne ɛkwaa mɔ so, ná ma mborohyɛen yɛ Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa manyamanya!’ ” Yiti Aarɔn tengyɛle ye sa wɔ Misraim nzue mɔ so, na mborohyɛen mɔ wale bɛɛyɛle Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa manyamanya.
Nakoso Misraim ngonyaayelɛfoɛ koso yele ngonyaa yɔle sɔ ala, na bɛmane mborohyɛen wale Misraim aseɛ so.
Afei Faro frɛle Mose ne Aarɔn sele bɛ kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔserɛ AWURADE bɛma ɔye mborohyɛen nemɔ ofi me ne me mmenia so, na ngɔma Yisraelfoɛ kɔhɔ ná baabɔ afɔleɛ bama AWURADE.” Na Mose sele Faro kyɛ, “Wɔ adaworoma, maa nwu mmerɛ horɛ bɔ nzrɛ ma wɔ, ɛne wɔ mbanyi mɔ ne wɔ mmenia, kyɛbɔ ɔkɔyɛ ná mborohyɛen nemɔ awuwu afi wɔ ne w’awuro mɔ so ɔ; asue Naele nu deɛ angome yeɛ ɔkɔha ɔ.” Na obuale kyɛ, “Ɛhema.” Na Mose koso hane kyɛ, “Ɔ́yɛ sɔ ala, kyɛbɔ aha ne, amaa ɔnate so anwu ye kyɛ ebiala nne berɛ bɔ ɔte kyɛ AWURADE yɛ Nyameɛ ne ɔ. Mborohyɛen nemɔ kofi wɔ ne w’awuro mɔ nu kɔhɔ, wɔ mbanyi ne wɔ mmenia so kɔhɔ, maa ɔkɔha bɛ bɔ bɛwɔ asue Naele nu angome.” Yiti Mose ne Aarɔn fili Faro nyunu berɛ bɛhɔle.
Na Mose srɛle AWURADE fale mborohyɛen bɔ wafa wawa Faro so ne nwo dwirɛ tole ye nyunu.
AWURADE yɔle bɔ Mose srɛle ye ne; mborohyɛen nemɔ wuwuli wɔ awuro nemɔ anu, aluo ne fieso.
Bɛboaboale bɛ noa kure kure, na maen ne anu bone mvamvamvamva.
Faro nwuni kyɛ bɛ nwo atɔ bɛ kãa, yiti obubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, na wandɛ bɛ so, kyɛbɔ AWURADE hane ne ala. Mvuture kakyi ngondia Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Ka kyire Aarɔn kyɛ, ‘Tengyɛ wɔ pɔmaa ne, ná fa fĩ aseɛnwo mvuture nu ma ɔkakyi ngondia wɔ Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa.’ ” Bɛyɔle sɔ.
Aarɔn tengyɛle ye sa nu fale pɔmaa ne fini aseɛnwo mvuture nu, na ngondia te guale mmenia ne ngaka so.
Na aseɛnwo mvuture amukoraa bɔ ɔwɔ Misraim kakyili ngondia.
Ngonyaayelɛfoɛ nemɔ bɔle mmɔden kyɛ bɛkɔma ngondia kɔwa ɔ, nakoso bangora.
Yiti ngondia kekale mmenia ne ngaka.
Na ngonyaayelɛfoɛ nemɔ sele Faro kyɛ, “Ɛhe de, Nyameɛ sa wɔ nu!
Nakoso Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, na wandɛ bɛ so, kyɛbɔ AWURADE hane ne ala. Nwɔsea pembepembe Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Dwɔso ngyerɛmɔ tutuutu kɔ Faro berɛ, wɔ mmerɛ bɔ ófite kɔ nzue ne anu ɔ, ná ka kyire ye kyɛ, ‘AWURADE nwa nyoo: Ma me mmenia nemɔ ate ma bɛhɔ, ná bɛɛso me.
Na sɛ amma me mmenia nemɔ ate ma bangɔ a, ngɔsoma nwɔsea pembepembe paa maa bɛkɔwa wɔ ne wɔ mbanyi ne wɔ mmenia so, ɔne w’awuro mɔ nu.
Nwɔsea koyi Misraimfoɛ awuro mɔ nu tɛkyɛ, ɔne aseɛ bɔ bɛ gya gyi so ne po.
Nakoso sɔ kyẽa ne, ngɔye Gosen aseɛ bɔ me mmenia te so ne ngosie ahameɛ; nwɔsea pembepembe paa ne ngɔhɔ berɛ bie, amaa ɔnate so anwu ye kyɛ me ole AWURADE wɔ aseɛ ye aso.
Yiti ngɔfa elelɛ ɛwɛen ngɔto me mmenia ne wɔ mmenia afia; na sɔ nzɛngyerɛnneɛ ne kosi ɛhema.’ ” AWURADE yɔle sɔ koso amba.
Nwɔsea pembepembe paa wale beeyili Faro awuro ne ye mbanyi mɔ awuro tɛkyɛ.
Na nwɔsea lele Misraim aseɛ ne aso amukoraa fale.
Afei Faro frɛle Mose ne Aarɔn, na osele bɛ kyɛ, “Ɛmɔhɔ bɛɛbɔ afɔleɛ bɛma ɛmɔ Nyameɛ ne wɔ maen he anu ala.” Na Mose buale kyɛ, “Ɔtte mayee kyɛ yɛkɔyɔ sɔ ɔ; ofikyɛ afɔleɛ bɔ yɛkɔbɔ kɔma AWURADE yɛ Nyameɛ nen, Misraimfoɛ bekyi.
Na sɛ yɛfa nningyein bɔ Misraimfoɛ bekyi yɛbɔ afɔleɛ wɔ bɛ nyunu wa a, aso bɛngɔboro yɛ nyɔboɛ?
Ɔsɛ kyɛ yɛpɛ atee bɔ bɛfa ɛlɛsa bɛpɛ ɔ wɔ ɛserɛ so yɛkɔbɔ afɔleɛ yɛma AWURADE yɛ Nyameɛ ne, kyɛbɔ wahyɛ yɛ ne ala.” Na Faro sele kyɛ, “Ngɔmaa ɛmɔkɔɔbɔ afɔleɛ bɛkɔma AWURADE ɛmɔ Nyameɛ ne wɔ ɛserɛ so, nakoso nnɛma ɛmɔkɔ dedeede.
Ɛ́mɔli me ti dwirɛ bɛma me.” Na Mose buale kyɛ, “Mefi wɔ wa mekɔ ala a, ngɔsrɛ AWURADE.
Na nwɔsea pembepembe paa ne kofi Faro ne ye mbanyi ne ye mmenia so kɔhɔ ɛhema.
Nakoso nnɛma Faro yɛ nnakannaka ko kyɛ ɔngɔma mmenia ne ngɔɔbɔ afɔleɛ ngɔma AWURADE.” Yiti Mose fili Faro nwo berɛ hɔle ɔɔsrɛle AWURADE.
AWURADE yɔle bɔ Mose srɛle ye ne.
Ɔmane nwɔsea pembepembe paa ne fili Faro ne ye mbanyi ne ye mmenia so hɔle, bɔ ko po anga berɛ ɔ. Nakoso Faro sá bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so sɔ mmerɛ ne, na wamma mmenia ne ate ma bangɔ.
Nyɛmmoa wuwuli Afei AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Kɔ Faro berɛ kose ye kyɛ, ‘AWURADE, Hebrifoɛ Nyameɛ ne nwa nyoo: Ma me mmenia nemɔ ate ma bɛhɔ, ná bɛɛsɔne me.
Ofikyɛ sɛ anyakyi bɛ ate ma bangɔ, ná ɛkye bɛ sie wa a, AWURADE tumi kɔma ngaka wue bɔ ye noa yɛ hye kɔha wɔ ngaka bɔ bahɔ adidie ɔ, wɔ mbɔngɔ mɔ, afunum mɔ, afupɔngɔ mɔ ne wɔ nyɛmmoa mɔ.
Nakoso AWURADE kɔfa ɛwɛen kɔto Yisrael ngaka ne Misraim ngaka b’afia, amaa ɔnate so Yisraelfoɛ ngaka nemɔ nu biala anwu.’ ” Na AWURADE hyɛle kyẽa kyɛ, “Ɛhema yeɛ AWURADE kɔyɔ sɔ nikyee ne wɔ aseɛ ne aso ɔ.” Aleɛ hyene ne, AWURADE yɔle sɔ ala. Misraimfoɛ nyɛmmoa mukoraa wuwuli, nakoso Yisraelfoɛ nyɛmmoa de, ko po anwu.
Faro somane mmenia maa bɛɛneane, na benwuni kyɛ Yisraelfoɛ ngaka nemɔ, nu ko po wanwu.
Nakoso Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, na wamma mmenia ne ate ma bangɔ.
Mbɔmbɔ anwonyerɛ to pete AWURADE sele Mose ne Aarɔn kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔfura foonoo nu nzoen bɛ sa bum ngoko, ná ma Mose ɔ́to hɔ anwuro wɔ Faro nyunu.
Ɔkɔkakyi mvuture muhumuhu kotu kɔfa Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa; na ɔkɔkakyi mbɔmbɔ kotutu mmenia ne ngaka nwo ngena wɔ Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa.” Yiti befurale foonoo nu nzoen, beegyinane Faro nyunu, Mose to hɔle anwuro, na ɔkakyili mbɔmbɔ tutuli mmenia ne ngaka nwo ngena.
Ɔnate mbɔmbɔ ne ati, ngonyaayelɛfoɛ nemɔ angora Mose nyunu gyina, ofikyɛ né mbɔmbɔ abobɔ ngonyaayelɛfoɛ nemɔ ne Misraimfoɛ amukoraa.
Nakoso AWURADE mane Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, na wandɛ bɛ so, kyɛbɔ AWURADE ha hyirele Mose ne ala. Asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Pɛ aleɛ dwɔso ná kɔ Faro berɛ kose ye kyɛ, ‘AWURADE, Hebrifoɛ Nyameɛ ne nwa nyoo: Ma me mmenia nemɔ ate ma bɛhɔ, na bɛɛsɔne me.
Ofikyɛ afei de, mebaama me hawo amukoraa ba wɔ bɔbɔ wɔ so, wɔ somvoɛ mɔ ne wɔ maen so, amaa ɔnate so anwu ye kyɛ ebiala nne berɛ bɔ ɔte kyɛ me ɔ wɔ aseɛ so amukoraa.
Na sɛ matengyɛ me sa mama ewue anwonyerɛ abɔ wɔ ne wɔ mmenia a, ahaa bekye awu afi aseɛ ye aso.
Nakoso mamaa anya wɔ ti adidi nu, kyɛ ngɔye me tumi ali ngohyire wɔ ɔ, amaa ɔnate so me dumaa atrɛ ahɔ aseɛ ye aso amukoraa.
Nakoso bekye po yeɛ adwɔso atia me mmenia, bɔ ɛngɔma bɛngɔhɔ ɔ.
Tie, ɛhema bekye sɔa ala, ngɔma asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ kɔtete kogua, bɔ ye sɛso ɔwwale Misraim le fite mmerɛ bɔ bɛkyekyele maen ne bɔ ɔbaadwu ɛnɛ ɔ. Yiti ma wɔ nyɛmmoa ne wɔ nikyee biala bɔ ɔwɔ buro bɛbra awuro bɛɛbɔ bɛ nwo waen, ofikyɛ asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ ne kɔtɔ kogua sona ne kaka bɔ ɔwɔ buro, bɔ wamma awuro so, na bekowuwu.’ ” Na Faro mbanyi nemɔ nu biala bɔ osuro AWURADE dwirɛ nen, ɔmane ye ngoaa ne ye nyɛmmoa nwatili wale awuro.
Nakoso bɛ nu biemɔ bɔ bemmu AWURADE dwirɛ ne de, bɛyakyili bɛ ngoaa ne bɛ nyɛmmoa mɔ wɔ eburo.
Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Tengyɛ wɔ sa fa kyire anwuro ma asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ tɔ gua Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa, ma ogua sona ne ngaka ne eburo mmakaa mukoraa so wɔ Misraim aseɛ so.” Yiti Mose pagyale ye pɔmaa ne hyirele anwuro, AWURADE mane anwuro bɔle nu kurudududu, ɔtɔle asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ guale, na agralaa tetele fili anwuro wale ase.
Na AWURADE tɔle asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ guale Misraim aseɛ so Asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ ne agralaa bɔ ɔ́tete see yerɛmyerɛm lili afra.
Na kyɛbɔ ye suronyi si te ne, ofite kyɛ Misraim yɛle maen ɔ, ye sɛso ɔwwale Misraim aseɛ ne amukoraa so le.
Asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ ne sɛkyele nikyee biala bɔ ɔwɔ buro wɔ Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa, fite mmenia so kodwu ngaka so; ɔsɛkyele eburo nningyein amukoraati, na ɔpombale eburo mmakaa mukoraati.
Sana Gosen aseɛ so, nekaa bɔ né Yisraelfoɛ te ne, yeɛ asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ ne bie andɔ berɛ ɔ. Afei Faro somane maa bɛɛfrɛle Mose ne Aarɔn bɛwale, na osele bɛ kyɛ, “Ɛhe de, mayɛ bɔne, AWURADE di be, na me ne me mmenia mukoraa yɛdi fɔ.
Yiti ɛ́mɔsrɛ AWURADE bɛma ɔyakyi, ofikyɛ agralaa ne asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ sɔa de, ɔbo yɛ so.
Ngɔma ɛmɔ kɔhɔ, na ɛmɔngɔtena wa ko.” Na Mose sele ye kyɛ, “Sɛ mefi kuro ye anu mefite pɛ a, ngɔtrɛ me sa nu ngɔsrɛ AWURADE, na agralaa ne kɔyakyi, yeɛ asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ ne koso ngɔte ngogua ko, amaa ɔnate so anwu ye kyɛ aseɛ ye te AWURADE deɛ.
Nakoso ɛne wɔ mbanyi mɔ de, mese kyɛ ɛmɔnnya bessurole AWURADE Nyameɛ.” Mose fili Faro awuro berɛ, ofili kuro ne anu, ɔtrɛle ye sa nu srɛle AWURADE, na agralaa ne asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ ne yakyili, na esue ne andɔ angua aseɛ ne aso ko.
Nakoso Faro nwuni kyɛ esue ne asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ ne agralaa ne ayakyi nen, ɔhɔle so yɔle bɔne, na ɔne ye mbanyi mɔ bebubuli mmakaa betuatuale bɛ so.
Yiti Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, na wamma Yisraelfoɛ nemɔ ate maa bangɔ, kyɛbɔ AWURADE nate Mose so hane ne ala.
Mmɛbɛ Afei AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Kɔ Faro berɛ, ofikyɛ me yeɛ mamaa ɔne ye mbanyi mɔ babubu mmakaa batuatua bɛ so ɔ, amaa ɔnate so mala me nzɛngyerɛnneɛ hemɔ ali wɔ bɛ berɛ.
Na ɔnate so ɛkɔha kyɛbɔ masi magoro Misraimfoɛ nwo, ɔne nzɛngyerɛnneɛ bɔ mayɔ ye bɛ berɛ kohyire ɛwa ne w’anomaa.
Na ɛhe kɔmaa ekonwu ye kyɛ me ole AWURADE.” Yiti Mose ne Aarɔn bɛhɔle Faro berɛ beesele ye kyɛ, “AWURADE, Hebrifoɛ Nyameɛ ne nwa nyoo, ‘Ɛkɔpo kyɛ ɛkɔbrɛ wɔ nwo ase wɔ me nyunu maa okoodwu kyinzu?
Ma me mmenia nemɔ ate ma bɛhɔ, ná bɛɛsɔne me.
Na sɛ ampene amma me mmenia nemɔ angɔ a, ɛhema ngɔma mmɛbɛ kɔwa wɔ maen ye anu, na bekoyi bɛkɔfa aseɛ ne, bɔ sona biala ngonwu aseɛ ne ɔ. Na nikyee biala bɔ ɔhale berɛ mane ɛmɔ, bɔ asukɔtwea nyɔboɛ ne anzɛkye ye ne, bekoli; yeɛ ɛmɔ mmakaa mukoraa bɔ begyigyi buro koso, bekoli.
Bekoyi w’awuro mɔ nu tɛkyɛ, wɔ mbanyi mɔ awuro amukoraa, ɔne Misraimfoɛ awuro amukoraa nu tɛkyɛ; bɔ wɔ baba mɔ ne wɔ nana mɔ bennwuni bie le, fite kyɛ bɛwale aseɛ ye aso bɔ ɔbaadwu ɛnɛ ɔ.’ ” Afei ɔkakyili ye nwo yakyili Faro berɛ hɔle.
Na Faro mbanyi mɔ sele ye kyɛ, “Kyinzu koraa yeɛ biaa he kosua yɛ ngaen maa ɔkɔɔpem ɔ?
Ma mmienzua ne bɛhɔ bɛɛsɔne AWURADE bɛ Nyameɛ ne.
Aso ennwu ye kyɛ Misraim abɔ ɔ?” Yiti bɛmane Mose ne Aarɔn sá wale Faro berɛ, na osele bɛ kyɛ, “Ɛmɔhɔ bɛɛsɔne AWURADE ɛmɔ Nyameɛ ne.
Nakoso ɛmɔ nu nwa mɔ yeɛ bɛkɔhɔ ɔ?” Na Mose sele kyɛ, “Yɛ ne yɛ ngwadaa ne yɛ mbanyi, yɛ mma mmienzua ne mmrasua, yɛ mmoaen ne yɛ nandwie mɔ yeɛ yɛkɔhɔ ɔ, ofikyɛ, ɔsɛ kyɛ yɛdi aluolue yɛhyɛ AWURADE animnyam.” Na Faro sele bɛ kyɛ, “AWURADE óli ɛmɔ si, sɛ ɔba ye kyɛ mema ate maa ɛmɔ ne ɛmɔ mma mɔ bɛkɔ a!
Yeɛ ɛmɔanwu ye kyɛ ɛmɔle adwene tɛɛ ɔ!
Ɔngɔyɛ yee!
Ɛ́mɔma mmienzua nemɔ angome bɛhɔ bɛɛsɔne AWURADE, ofikyɛ bɔ ɛmɔpena hɔ ɛne.” Yiti bɛfoane Mose ne Aarɔn befili Faro nyunu.
Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Ma wɔ sa so kyire Misraim aseɛ ne ma mmɛbɛ beyi bɛfa aseɛ ne, ná beli aseɛ ne aso nyaanyaa mukoraa bɔ asukɔtwea akungumaboɔ ne anzɛkye ye ne.” Yiti Mose mane ye pɔmaa ne aso hyirele Misraim aseɛ ne.
Na AWURADE mane eyia afiteleɛ mvrama tuli aseɛ ne aso sɔ kyẽa ne eyia ne kɔngɔen amukoraa.
Na aleɛ hyene ngyerɛmɔ nen, né eyia afiteleɛ mvrama ne afa mmɛbɛ nemɔ wawa.
Mmɛbɛ nemɔ wale Misraim aseɛ so amu, na beyi bɛfale Misraim maen ne amu.
Na kyɛbɔ besi bɛyɛle manyamanya nen, ebie ɔwwale le, yeɛ ebie koso ngɔwa le.
Beyili bɛfale aseɛ ne aso amukoraa mane aseɛ ne aso yɛle tunn.
Na aseɛ ne aso nyaa mukoraa ne mmakaammaa mukoraa bɔ asukɔtwea akungumaboɔ ne anzɛkye bɛ ne, belili.
Nikyee monɛ ko po anga wɔ eburo mmakaa ne ndire mɔ so, wɔ Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa.
Afei Faro hane ye nwo tole ye sa frɛle Mose ne Aarɔn maa bɛwale, na osele kyɛ, “Mayɛ bɔne matia AWURADE ɛmɔ Nyameɛ ne, ɔne ɛmɔ.
Yiti mesrɛ wɔ, ɛhe angome de, fa me bɔne kyɛ me; na ɛ́mɔsrɛ AWURADE ɛmɔ Nyameɛ ne ma ɔye ewue he fi me so.” Yiti Mose fili Faro nwo berɛ hɔle ɔɔsrɛle AWURADE.
Na AWURADE mane eyia atɔleɛ mvrama piri bie tuli, na opiane mmɛbɛ nemɔ ooguale Ɛpo Kɔkorɛ nu.
Abɛbɛ ko po anga berɛ wɔ Misraim aseɛ so nekaa biala.
Nakoso AWURADE mane Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, na wamma Yisraelfoɛ ate ma bangɔ.
Afei AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Tengyɛ wɔ sa fa kyire anwuro ma awosii bra Misraim aseɛ so, awosii bɔ sana bɛfa bɛ sa befuafua ɔ.” Yiti Mose tengyɛle ye sa hyirele anwuro, na awosii kabii wale Misraim aseɛ so amukoraa ɛlɛsa.
Ɛlɛsa mumua, ebiala annwu obiɛngo, anaakyɛ wandu ye gya; nakoso nekaa bɔ né Yisraelfoɛ bɛte ne de, ewienu yɛle hyireinn.
Afei Faro frɛle Mose, na osele ye kyɛ, “Ɛmɔhɔ bɛɛsɔne AWURADE ɛmɔ ne ɛmɔ mma mɔ bɛhɔ; nakoso ɛmɔ mmoaen ne nandwie mɔ de, odi kyɛ bɛka wa.” Nakoso Mose sele kyɛ, “Odi kyɛ ɛma yɛ sa ka nningyein bɔ yɛkɔfa kɔbɔ afɔleɛ ɔne naen yeralɛ afɔleɛ yɛkɔma AWURADE yɛ Nyameɛ ne ɔ. Odi kyɛ yɛfa yɛ nyɛmmoa koso yɛkɔ; bɛ gya mbaboa ko po ngɔha wa, ofikyɛ bɛ nu bie yeɛ yɛkwaafa yɛsɔne AWURADE yɛ Nyameɛ ɔ. Na yɛngɔhora ngonwu nikyee bɔ yɛkɔfa yɛkɔsɔne AWURADE ɔ, sana yadwu dɔ koraka.” Nakoso AWURADE mane Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, na wamma bɛ ate maa bangɔ.
Na Faro sele Mose kyɛ, “Fi me nyunu wa kɔ!
Nea wɔ nwo yé, na nnɛmaa menwu wɔ nyunu ko; ofikyɛ kyẽa bɔ ɛkɔwa me nyunu ne, ngɔmaa bekohu wɔ.” Na Mose buale kyɛ, “Yoo, ɛnwa nnɛmaa meba wɔ nyunu ko a, mate!”
Amaneɛ piri bɔ ɔpɛ ye bo ɔ AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Waha amaneɛ pirikua ko bɔ mebaafa meto Faro ne Misraim so ɔ. Ɛhe asi ye, ɔkɔmaa ɛmɔkofi wa bɛkɔhɔ, na sɛ ɔma ɛmɔ ate a, ɔkɔfoa ɛmɔ maa ɛmɔkofi wa.
Afei, bɔ wɔ mmenia nemɔ amaneɛ kyɛ, ɔsɛ kyɛ bienzua biala ne brasua biala obisa ɛdwetɛ ne sikaa kɔkorɛ mbembenanneɛ ofi obiɛngo Misraimniɛ berɛ.” AWURADE mane Misraimfoɛ lole Yisraelfoɛ.
Asa koso, né Mose te sona bɔ odi mu wɔ Misraim aseɛ so, wɔ Faro mbanyi mɔ ne maen ne nyunu.
Na Mose hane kyɛ, “AWURADE nwa nyoo: Ngɔɔnatenate Misraim kɔyɛ abunnamu; na bamuɛbaa bienzua biala bɔ ɔwɔ Misraim aseɛ so kowu, fite Faro bamuɛbaa bienzua bɔ ɔtena ye bia so ɔ so, kodwu afaneɛ bɔ osi aburoo ɔ ɔwa so, ɔne nyɛmmoa mɔ bɛ bamuɛbaa mɔ so.
Na awuye piri paa bɔ bɛkɔbɔ ye wɔ Misraim aseɛ mukoraa so ne, ebie ossili le, yeɛ ebie koso ngosi ko.
Nakoso Yisraelfoɛ mɔ de, kyea po ongopo sona anaa kaka biala; amaa ɔnate so ɛmɔanwu ye kyɛ AWURADE ma nzonzoleɛ da Misraim ne Yisrael nu.
Na wɔ mbanyi hemɔ amukoraa bɛkɔwa me nyunu bekoobu ndwerɛ bɛkɔhã kyɛ, ‘Fi wa kɔ, ɛne wɔ mmenia bɔ beli wɔ si amukoraa!’ Na ɛhe asi ne, ngofi wa ngɔhɔ.” Afei Mose fɛle ɛyaa hahii fili Faro nyunu berɛ hɔle.
Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Faro ngɔtɛ ɛmɔ so, na ɔnate so m’anwanwadeɛ kɔsone pee wɔ Misraim aseɛ so.” Mose ne Aarɔn yɔle anwanwadeɛ he amukoraa wɔ Faro nyunu; AWURADE mane Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, na wamma Yisraelfoɛ ate ma bamvi ye aseɛ so bangɔ.
Abɔtra aluolue ne AWURADE sele Mose ne Aarɔn wɔ Misraim aseɛ so kyɛ, “Bosome he yeɛ ɔkɔyɛ ɛmɔ bosome bɔ oli moa ɔ; ɔkɔyɛ afoɛ ne anu bosome bɔ oli moa kɔma ɛmɔ.
Ka kyire Yisrael maen ne amukoraa kyɛ, bosome he anu kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so buru ne, ɔsɛ kyɛ bienzua biala pena boaen akrɔngrɔma ko ma ye awuro ama, awuro biala nu kohia boaen akrɔngrɔma ko.
Na sɛ boaen akrɔngrɔma ne bo awuro ne anu mmenia so a, ye de ma sɔ awuro ne ɔne awuro foforɛ bɔ opingye ye ne bɛhyɛ naen ne, kyɛbɔ nu mmenia somaa si te ɔ. Na kyɛbɔ sona biala kɔhora ye di ne, sɔ yeɛ ɛ́mɔnea so bɛ́fa mmoaen akrɔngrɔma ne ɔ. Ɔsɛ kyɛ boaen akrɔngrɔma ne yɛ nyii bɔ wali afoɛ ko, bɔ ollili nnɛen ɔ. Ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛmɔsa nu bɛye bɛ befi mmoaen anaa mbɔngye nemɔ anu.
Ɛ́mɔfa ye bésie toonn ma odwu bosome he anu kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so buru ne nna ne, na afei Yisrael maen ne amukoraa behũhũ bɛ mmoaen ne nɔsoa.
Awuro bɔ bekoli naen ne wɔ nu nen, ɔsɛ kyɛ bɛfa mogya ne bie bɛkeka aponnwaa nyɔ ne, ɔne sua ne ye bati so.
Ɔsɛ kyɛ bɛtoto naen ne bedi ye sɔ kɔngɔen ne, ná bɛfa paanoo kabrɛdi ne awɔwee nyaa bɛboka so.
Nnɛma ɛmɔdi ye monɛ, yeɛ nnɛma ɛmɔfa nzue bɛto, na mmom ɛ́mɔtoto: ye ti, ye gya ne ye kunu nningyein ne boka so.
Nnɛma ɛmɔfa ebie besie ma aleɛ kye so; na sɛ ebie ka ma aleɛ kye so a, odi kyɛ ɛmɔyera ye.
Atee he aso yeɛ ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛmɔpe so bedi ɔ: ɛ́mɔbɔ ɛmɔ abɔsoɛ, ɛ́mɔwura ɛmɔ mbaboa, ɛ́mɔfa ɛmɔ pɔmaa nemɔ bétiratira, ná ɛ́mɔli ye ndɛndɛ.
AWURADE Abɔtra ne ɛne.
Ngɔɔpɛ nu Misraim aseɛ so sɔ kyẽa ne kɔngɔen, na ngohũ Misraim aseɛ so bamuɛbaa mukoraa, fite mmenia so kodwu ngaka so; na ngobua Misraim mmosoen amukoraa ndɛen.
Me ole AWURADE.
Mogya ne yeɛ ɔkɔhyɛ ɛmɔ nzorɛ, wɔ awuro mɔ bɔ ɛmɔtete nu ne anu ɔ. Na sɛ menwu mogya ne a, ngɔbɔ ngɔtra ɛmɔ, amaa sɛ mébɔ Misraim maen ne a, amaneɛ ne bie ando ɛmɔ.
Kyẽa sɔ ne kɔyɛ ngayeɛ kyẽa kɔma ɛmɔ, na ɛ́mɔli ye aluolue bɛma AWURADE; na odi kyɛ ɛmɔdi sɔ aluolue ne afebɔɔ wɔ ɛmɔ aworɛ ndoatoasoɛ mukoraa nu.
Paanoo Kabrɛdi aluolue “Ɛmɔkoli paanoo kabrɛdi ɛlɛsoo.
Kyẽa bɔ oli moa ne, ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛmɔye mɔle harewaa biala befi ɛmɔ awuro mɔ nu, ofikyɛ ofi kyẽa bɔ oli moa ne alaa bɔ ɔkwaadwu kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so nzoo nen, sona biala bɔ okoli mɔle harewaa ne, bɛkɔpɛ ye asue bekofi Yisraelfoɛ nu.
Ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛmɔyɛ nyianu krongron wɔ kyẽa bɔ oli moa ne, yeɛ kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so nzoo ne koso ɛ́mɔyɛ nyianu krongron.
Nnɛma ɛmɔyɔ adwuma wɔ sɔ ngyẽa ne; sana aleɛ bɔ ebiala koli angome yeɛ ɛ́mɔyɔ ye nwo adwuma ɔ. Ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛmɔdi Paanoo Kabrɛdi aluolue ne, ofikyɛ sɔ kyẽa ne yeɛ nyele ɛmɔ amukoraati mvili Misraim aseɛ so ɔ. Yiti ɛ́mɔtu sɔ kyẽa ne besie berɛ beli sɔ aluolue ne afebɔɔ wɔ ɛmɔ aworɛ ndoatoasoɛ mukoraa nu.
Bosome bɔ oli moa ne anu, kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so buru ne nna ne ye nɔsoa, bɔ ɔkwaadwu kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so aburanyɔ ne ko ne ye nɔsoa, ɛ́mɔli paanoo kabrɛdi.
Ɛlɛsoo ne anu, ɔnzɛ kyɛ benwu mɔle harewaa wɔ ɛmɔ awuro; ofikyɛ ebiala bɔ okoli mɔle harewaa nen, sɛ ɛwɔfoɛ ahɔ oo, anaa bɛwole ye maen ne anu oo, bɛkɔpɛ sɔ sona ne asue bekofi Yisraelfoɛ nu.
Nnɛma ɛmɔdi nikyee harewaa biala.
Ɛ́mɔli paanoo kabrɛdi wɔ nekaa biala bɔ ɛmɔkɔtena ɔ.” Abɔtra Aluolue bɔ oli moa Afei Mose frɛle Yisrael mbanyi amukoraa, na osele bɛ kyɛ, “Ebiala ɔɔhye boaen ko ma ye awuro ama, ná ohu ye fa yɛ Abɔtra boaen ne.
Ɛ́mɔfa sufiɛ, ná ɛ́mɔfa bɛbɔ mogya bɔ ɔwɔ ayaa ne anu, ná ɛ́mɔfa mogya bɔ ɔwɔ nu ne bɛ́keka sua ne bati so ɔne aponnwaa nyɔ ne.
Nnɛma ɛmɔ nu biala fi ye awuro fite maa okodwu ngyerɛmɔ.
Ofikyɛ AWURADE kɔɔpɛ nu kohũhũ Misraimfoɛ; na sɛ AWURADE nwu mogya bɔ ɔwɔ sua ne ye bati so, ɔne aponnwaa nyɔ nemɔ nwo a, okosã sɔ anoa ne anwo, na ɔngɔma sɛkyelɛniɛ ne ate ma ɔngɔwa ɛmɔ awuro berɛ ongohũhũ ɛmɔ.
Odi kyɛ ɛmɔdi sɔ dwirɛ he aso; ɔte nhyehyɛleɛ ma wɔ ne wɔ boso ama afebɔɔ.
Na sɛ ɛmɔdwu aseɛ bɔ AWURADE baafa ma ɛmɔ ne aso, kyɛbɔ wahyɛ ye nwo bɔ ne a, ɛmɔhɔ so beli sɔ aluolue he.
Na sɛ ɛmɔ mma mɔ bisa ɛmɔ kyɛ, ‘Ɛmɔ aluolue he, ye bo ole sɛɛ?’ a Ɛmɔhã kyɛ, ‘Ɔte Abɔtra afɔleɛ bɔ yɛbɔ yɛma AWURADE bɔ ohuhuni Misraimfoɛ ne.
Nakoso odwuli Yisraelfoɛ awuro mɔ nwo wɔ Misraim nen, ɔpɛle nu hɔle maa yɛnyane yɛ ti yɛdidili nu.’ ” Na mmenia ne bɔle bɛ ti ase bɛsɔne (Nyameɛ).
Na Yisraelfoɛ mɔ hɔle bɛɛyɔle sɔ, kyɛbɔ AWURADE hyɛle Mose ne Aarɔn ne ala. Misraim bamuɛbaa mmienzua wuwu Ye abunnamu ne, AWURADE huhuni Misraim aseɛ so bamuɛbaa mmienzua mukoraati, fite Faro bamuɛbaa bienzua bɔ ɔtena ye bia so ɔ so, kodwu sona bɔ bahye ye nnure bawura kuku nu ye bamuɛbaa so, ɔne nyɛmmoa mɔ bɛ bamuɛbaa mɔ so.
Yeɛ Faro dwɔsole kɔngɔen ne, ɔne ye mbanyi mɔ amukoraa ne Misraimfoɛ amukoraa, na awuyebɔlɛ piri paa wale Misraim, ofikyɛ awuro biala nne berɛ bɔ sona anwu nu ɔ. Na Faro tole ye sa frɛle Mose ne Aarɔn kɔngɔen ne sele bɛ kyɛ, “Ɛmɔ ne Yisraelfoɛ, ɛmɔhã bɛ nwo befi me maen ye anu bɛhɔ!
Ɛmɔhɔ bɛɛsɔne AWURADE, kyɛbɔ ɛmɔaha ne.
Ɛ́mɔfa ɛmɔ mmoaen ne ɛmɔ nandwie mɔ, ná ɛ́mɔfi wa bɛhɔ, kyɛbɔ ɛmɔhane nen, ná ɛ́mɔyira me koso.
Misraimfoɛ hane Yisraelfoɛ bo kyɛ bɛha bɛ nwo befi aseɛ ne aso; ofikyɛ bɛhane kyɛ, “Yɛ mukoraa yawu yayie.” Yiti Yisraelfoɛ tetele bɛ mɔle wɔ mmerɛ bɔ né ɔngeka ɔ. Bɛfale bɛ ndena bɛkyekyele ye nwo wɔ ngukue nu, na bɛfa bɛtole bɛ kɔme anwo.
Yisraelfoɛ yɔle kyɛbɔ Mose ha hyirele bɛ ne, ofikyɛ né badide ɛdwetɛ ne sikaa kɔkorɛ mbembenanneɛ ne ɛtena bafi Misraimfoɛ berɛ.
Né AWURADE ama Misraimfoɛ alo Yisraelfoɛ dada; yiti bɛ sa hane bɔ bebisale befili bɛ berɛ amukoraati.
Bɛyɛle Misraimfoɛ dosodoso.
Yisraelfoɛ tu fi Misraim Yisraelfoɛ tu fili Ramese bɛhɔle Sukote.
Mmienzua kɔyɛ apee ɛyaa nzia yeɛ bɛfale ase bɛhɔle ɔ; banga mmrasua ne ngwadaa bammoka so.
Mmenia mvrafra pee koso ne bɛ hɔle, na nyɛmmoa pee paa boka so: mmoaen ne nandwie.
Na mɔle kabrɛdi bɔ bɛ ne ye fili Misraim wale ne, bɛfa bɛyɔle taterɛ.
Nna mɔle harewaa ɔ. Na ɔnate kyɛ betuli bɛ apereapereɛ so befili Misraim ne ati, bannya atee banyɔ aleɛ bɔ bekoli ye atunu ɔ. Yisraelfoɛ afoɛ bɔ belili wɔ Misraim te ɛyaa nna ne aburasa.
Na kyẽa bɔ afoɛ ɛyaa nna ne aburasa ne sone ne, AWURADE mmenia ne amukoraa tu fili Misraim aseɛ so.
Sɔ kɔngɔen ne, AWURADE lili Yisraelfoɛ nwo afofi, kyɛbɔ ɔkɔyɛ bɔ ɔkɔye bɛ kofi Misraim aseɛ so ɔ. Yiti odwu sɔ kyẽa ne kɔngɔen a, Yisraelfoɛ aworɛ ndoatoasoɛ amukoraa besili pɛ bɛfa bɛye AWURADE ayɛ.
Abɔtra ne nwo nhyehyɛleɛ Na AWURADE sele Mose ne Aarɔn kyɛ, “Abɔtra ne nwo nhyehyɛleɛ ɛhe: amanvraniɛ biala nni ye aleɛ ne bie.
Nakoso kanganiɛ biala bɔ afa sikaa atɔ ye ne, ɛpɛ ye bienzua de a, ɔkora di bie.
Ɛwɔfoɛ bɔ ɔne ɛmɔ baatena anaa paaniɛ biala nni bie.
Awuro ko anu ala yeɛ odi kyɛ ɛmɔtena bedi ɔ; nnɛma ɛmɔfa naen ne bie befite aluo, yeɛ nnɛma ɛmɔbɔ ye bowue nu.
Ɔsɛ kyɛ Yisraelfoɛ mukoraati bedi sɔ aluolue ne.
Na sɛ ɛwɔfoɛ bie ɔne wɔ yeɛ bɛte ɔ, ná okuro kyɛ odi Abɔtra aluolue ne ɔye AWURADE ayɛ a, ye de maa bɛpɛ ye nwo ama mmienzua mukoraa bɛ bienzua, amaa wanya ye nwo ate wali bie.
Ɛhe kɔmaa ɔkɔyɛ kyɛ maen ne anu niɛ; nakoso bɔ bɛppɛle ye bienzua ne de, ɔnzɛ kyɛ odi bie.
Mmeraa komapɛ bɔ ɔwɔ berɛ ma maen mmaa ne, ye ala yeɛ ɔwɔ berɛ ma ɛwɔfoɛ bɔ ɔne ɛmɔ baatena ɔ.” Yiti Yisraelfoɛ amukoraa yɔle kyɛbɔ AWURADE hyɛle Mose ne Aarɔn ne ala. Na AWURADE yele Yisraelfoɛ ɛlɔen kure kure ne fili Misraim aseɛ so sɔ kyẽa ne.
Bɛfa bamuɛbaa bienzua bɛma Nyameɛ AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Tu bamuɛbaa mukoraa sie berɛ ma me; ebiala bɔ okoli moa kofi koɛsɛen nu kɔwa wɔ Yisraelfoɛ nu ne, sona oo, ayɛmmoa oo, ɔte me deɛ.” Paanoo Kabrɛdi aluolue Na Mose sele mmenia ne kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔkaye sɔ kyẽa he bɔ ɛmɔfili Misraim ɔ, bɔ ɛmɔfili ngoaasolɛ nu ne, ofikyɛ AWURADE nate tumi piri so yeɛ ɔyele ɛmɔ fili Misraim ɔ; yiti nnɛma ɛmɔdi paanoo harewaa biala.
Ɛnɛ kyẽa ye, wɔ bosome Abibo nu, yeɛ ɛ́mɔfi Misraim ɔ. Na sɛ AWURADE fa wɔ kodwu Kanaanfoɛ, Hitifoɛ, Amorifoɛ, Hiwifoɛ ne Yebusifoɛ aseɛ bɔ ɔtale ndaen hyirele wɔ nana mɔ kyɛ ɔkɔfa kɔma wɔ ne aso, aseɛ bɔ nyɔfonesue ne woɛ tengyɛ wɔ so ne aso a, di aluolue he wɔ ɛsraen he anu.
Di paanoo kabrɛdi ɛlɛsoo, ná di aluolue ne fa ye AWURADE ayɛ wɔ ye ɛlɛsoo ne aso.
Ɛlɛsoo yeɛ ɛ́mɔli paanoo kabrɛdi ɔ; ɔnzɛ kyɛ benwu paanoo harewaa biala wɔ ɛmɔ berɛ, anaa mɔle harewaa wɔ ɛmɔ aseɛ so nekaa biala.
Na sɔ kyẽa ne, kyire nu kyire ɛwa kyɛ, ‘Ɔnate nikyee bɔ AWURADE yɔ mane me wɔ mmerɛ bɔ mvili Misraim ne ati ɔ.’ Na ɛhe kɔyɛ kyɛ sɛngyerɛnneɛ bɔ ɔwɔ wɔ sa nwo, ná wayɛ ngayeɛ wɔ wɔ nwoma so wama wɔ, amaa ɔnate so AWURADE mmeraa ne ala wɔ noa; ofikyɛ AWURADE nate tumi piri so yeɛ ɔyele wɔ fili Misraim ɔ. Yiti di sɔ nhyehyɛleɛ he aso wɔ ye mmerɛ so afoɛnoa biala.
Bamuɛbaa bienzua Na sɛ AWURADE fa wɔ kodwu Kanaanfoɛ aseɛ so, ná ɔfa ma wɔ, kyɛbɔ ɔtale ndaen hyirele wɔ ne wɔ nana mɔ ne a, tu abɔdeɛ biala bɔ okoli moa kofi koɛsɛen nu kɔwa ne sie berɛ ma AWURADE.
Wɔ nyɛmmoa mɔ bɛ bamuɛbaa bienzua mukoraa te AWURADE deɛ.
Fa boaen ba sesã afunum bamuɛbaa biala, nakoso sɛ anzesã ye de a, ye de bu afunum ne kɔme anu.
Yeɛ wɔ mma mɔ bɛ nu bamuɛbaa bienzua biala koso, odi kyɛ ɛpɔ ye fi AWURADE berɛ.
Na sɛ kyẽa bie ɛwa bisa wɔ kyɛ, “Ɛhe bo kyire sɛɛ’ a, wɔ koso abua ye kyɛ, ‘AWURADE nate ye tumi piri so yeɛ ɔyele yɛ fili Misraim ngoaasolɛ nu ɔ. Ofikyɛ mmerɛ bɔ Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so kyɛ ɔngɔma yɛngɔhɔ nen, AWURADE huhuni Misraim aseɛ so bamuɛbaa mukoraati, fite mmenia bamuɛbaa mɔ so, maa oodwuli nyɛmmoa bamuɛbaa mɔ so.
Na ɔnate sɔ ati yeɛ mefa kaka bamuɛbaa bienzua biala mebɔ afɔleɛ mema AWURADE ɔ. Nakoso me mma mɔ bɛ nu bamuɛbaa bienzua biala de, mepɔ ye (mefi AWURADE berɛ).’ Na ɛhe kɔyɛ kyɛ sɛngyerɛnneɛ bɔ ɔwɔ wɔ sa nwo, anaa ngayeɛ wɔ wɔ nwoma so, ofikyɛ AWURADE nate tumi piri so yeɛ ɔyele yɛ fili Misraim ɔ.” Munungum ningɔnn ne see ningɔnn Faro mane mmenia ne ate kyɛ bɛhɔ nen, Nyameɛ amva bɛ amva Filistifoɛ aseɛ so, ɔwɔ nu kyɛ né berɛ yeɛ ɔte tika ɔ. Ofikyɛ Nyameɛ hane kyɛ, “Sɛ mmenia ne kɔtɔ koɛ nu a, annea a né banu bɛ nwo, ná basa bahɔ Misraim.” Yiti ɛserɛ so atee bɔ ɔkɔ Ɛpo Kɔkorɛ nwo ne, Nyameɛ mane mmenia ne makye fale so.
Na Yisraelfoɛ tu fili Misraim aseɛ so bɛhɔle kyɛ mmenia bɔ bɛ́kɔ koɛ ɔ. Mose sesale Yosef mmowue ne hɔle; ofikyɛ né Yosef ama Yisrael mma nemɔ ata ndaen.
Osele kyɛ, “Nyameɛ koogyina ɛmɔ si, na ɔyɛ a, ɛ́mɔfa me mmowue ne béfi wa bɛhɔ.” Betuli bɛ bo befili Sukote, na beesikyele Etam, wɔ ɛserɛ ne noa.
Alehyeleɛ nu, AWURADE lili bɛ nyunu wɔ munungum ningɔnn nu hyirele bɛ atee.
Na alesaleɛ nu koso, ɔtale hyireinn mane bɛ wɔ see ningɔnn nu, kyɛbɔ bɛkɔhora bɛkɔnate eyia ne kɔngɔen ɔ. Munungum ningɔnn bɔ né oli bɛ nyunu ne, wanyakyi bɛ nu eyia; yeɛ see ningɔnn ne koso wanyakyi bɛ nu kɔngɔen.
Bɛpɛ Ɛpo Kɔkorɛ ne Afei AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Ka kyire Yisraelfoɛ kyɛ besa bɛ si beesi asikyeleɛ wɔ Pi Hahirote nyunu, wɔ Migidol ne ɛpo ne b’afia, wɔ Baal Sefon nyunu.
Ye ndendeneɛ so yeɛ ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛmɔsi asikyeleɛ ne ɔ, wɔ ɛpo ne anoa.
Ofikyɛ Faro kɔha kɔfa Yisraelfoɛ nwo kyɛ, ‘Baaha aseɛ ne aso, na ɛserɛ ne amaa basota berɛ.’ Ngɔma Faro kobubu mmakaa kotua ye so.
Ɔkɔpo bɛ so, nakoso ɔnate Faro ne ye lɔen amukoraa so ngɔhyɛ me nwo animnyam; na Misraimfoɛ konwu ye kyɛ me ole AWURADE.” Na sɔ ala yeɛ Yisraelfoɛ yɔle ɔ. Mmerɛ bɔ bɛha behyirele Misraim hene kyɛ mmenia nemɔ anwati nen, ɔne ye mbanyi mɔ benyane adwene foforɛ wɔ mmenia nemɔ anwo, na besele kyɛ, “Nzikyɛ nikye yeɛ yayɔ ye, bɔ yama Yisraelfoɛ ayakyi yɛ solɛ ná bahɔ ye?” Yiti osiesiele ye teaseɛnam, na ɔfale ye asraafoɛ bokale ye nwo so.
Ɔfale teaseɛnam paa paa ɛyaa nzia, ɔne Misraim teaseɛnam amukoraati, bɔ né safohene mɔ tete ye mukoraa nu ɔ. Na AWURADE mane Misraim hene Faro bubuli mmakaa tuale ye so, yiti ɔpole Yisraelfoɛ so, wɔ mmerɛ bɔ né Yisraelfoɛ nate atunu bɛ́kɔ ngonimlilɛ so ɔ. Misraimfoɛ pole bɛ so: Faro mbɔngɔ mɔ ne teaseɛnam amukoraa, ye pɔngɔhanɛfoɛ ne ye asraafoɛ amukoraa, na bɛɛtole bɛ kyɛ basi asikyeleɛ wɔ ɛpo ne noa wɔ Pi Hahirote, wɔ Baal Sefon nyunu.
Na mmerɛ bɔ Faro pingyele bɛ ne, Yisraelfoɛ mane bɛ nye so, na benwuni kyɛ Misraimfoɛ bɛ́po bɛ so; yiti ɛserɛ piri hane Yisraelfoɛ nemɔ, na besu bɛfrɛle AWURADE.
Na besele Mose kyɛ, “Asieleɛ mɔ nne Misraim hɔ ɔ, bɔ yiti yeɛ afa yɛ awa kyɛ yɛɛwuwu yɛgua ɛserɛ ye aso ye?
Ɛɛyele yɛ fili Misraim ne, bɔ amaa wato yɛ hɔ ɛne?
Anaa yanga yangyire wɔ wɔ Misraim kyɛ, “Yakyi yɛ konn ma yɛso Misraimfoɛ’?
Ofikyɛ, sɛ yɛso Misraimfoɛ mmom a, ahaa ɔte paa tra kyɛ yɛkowuwu ɛserɛ so ɔ!” Na Mose sele mmenia ne kyɛ, “Nnɛma ɛmɔsuro, ɛ́mɔgyina pindinn, ná ɛ́mɔnea ngoalelɛ bɔ AWURADE kole ɛmɔ ɛnɛ ɔ; ofikyɛ Misraimfoɛ bɔ ɛmɔnwu bɛ ɛnɛ ye, ɛmɔngonwu bɛ ko le.
AWURADE kɔho kɔma ɛmɔ, yiti ɛmɔ de, ɛ́mɔyɛ konn.” Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Nzu ati yeɛ esu frɛ me ye?
Ka kyire Yisraelfoɛ kyɛ bɛhɔ bɛ nyunu.
Ma wɔ pɔmaa ne aso, ná tengyɛ wɔ sa ɛpo ne aso ma nu hyɛ nyɔ, amaa ɔnate so Yisraelfoɛ afa aseɛ wosee so bapɛ ɛpo ne.
Me de, ngɔma Misraimfoɛ kobubu mmakaa kotua bɛ so, amaa ɔnate so bapo Yisraelfoɛ so.
Na ɔnate Faro ne ye asraafoɛ amukoraa so, ye teaseɛnam mɔ ne ye pɔngɔhanɛfoɛ so, ngɔhyɛ me nwo animnyam.
Na sɛ ɔnate Faro ne ye teaseɛnam mɔ, ɔne ye pɔngɔhanɛfoɛ so mehyɛ me nwo animnyam a, Misraimfoɛ konwu ye kyɛ me ole AWURADE.” Afei Nyameɛ abɔfo bɔ né oli Yisrael ɛlɔen ne nyunu ne, ɔse oolili bɛ si.
Na munungum ningɔnn ne fili bɛ nyunu oolili bɛ si, na oogyinane Misraim ɛlɔen ne Yisrael ɛlɔen b’afia.
Na kɔngɔen ne amukoraa, munungum ne yɛle awosii mane bue ko, yeɛ ɔtale mane bue ko; yiti bue ko ne angora ambingye obiɛngo kɔngɔen ne.
Afei Mose tengyɛle ye sa ɛpo ne aso.
Na AWURADE mane eyia afiteleɛ mvrama piri bie tuli, na oopiane ɛpo ne sale nziɛ kɔngɔen ne.
Ɔmane ɛpo ne kakyili aseɛ wosee, na nzue ne anu hyɛle.
Na Yisraelfoɛ fale aseɛ wosee so pɛle ɛpo ne; na nzue ne yɛle ɛwaen mane bɛ wɔ bɛ famaa so ne bɛ bɛen so.
Misraimfoɛ pole bɛ so.
Faro mbɔngɔ mɔ, ye teaseɛnam ne ye pɔngɔhanɛfoɛ amukoraa belili bɛ si bɛhɔle ɛpo ne afia.
Na alebahyene ne, AWURADE tole ye nye fale see ningɔnn ne munungum ne anu neane Misraim asraafoɛ ne, na ɔmane Misraim asraafoɛ nemɔ nye so tanene bɛ.
Ɔmane bɛ teaseɛnam nemɔ gya sɛkyesɛkyele bɔ né bɛngora ndɛ kɔ ɔ. Yiti Misraimfoɛ sele kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔma yɛ́nwati yɛ́fi Yisraelfoɛ mɔ nwo wa, ofikyɛ AWURADE gyi bɛ si ɔko tia Misraim.” Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Tengyɛ wɔ sa wɔ ɛpo ne aso ma nzue ne sá ha bɔ nu, ná obu fa Misraimfoɛ ne bɛ teaseɛnam mɔ ne bɛ pɔngɔhanɛfoɛ so.” Yiti Mose tengyɛle ye sa wɔ ɛpo ne aso, na aleɛ baahye ne, ɛpo nzue ne sá wale ye boso.
Na Misraimfoɛ bɛ́nwati bɛ́kɔ nen, AWURADE hane bɛ guale ɛpo ne anu wɔ asufia.
Nzue ne ha tuale, na ɔfale teaseɛnam nemɔ, pɔngɔhanɛfoɛ nemɔ, ɔne Faro ɛlɔen amukoraa bɔ bɛpole Yisraelfoɛ so wɔ ɛpo ne anu ne.
Bɛ nu ko po anga.
Nakoso Yisraelfoɛ de, bɛfale aseɛ wosee so bɛpɛle ɛpo ne wɔ ye afia; na nzue ne yɛle ɛwaen mane bɛ wɔ bɛ famaa so ne bɛ bɛen so.
Yiti AWURADE lele Yisraelfoɛ fili Misraimfoɛ sa nu sɔ kyẽa ne; na Yisraelfoɛ nwuni Misraimfoɛ kyɛ bawuwu bagua mboanoa berɛ.
Yisraelfoɛ nwuni tumi piri bɔ AWURADE fa ho tiale Misraimfoɛ ne.
Yiti Yisraelfoɛ surole AWURADE, na belele AWURADE ne ye somvoɛ Mose belili.
Mose ne Yisraelfoɛ edwein ne Afei Mose ne Yisraelfoɛ tole edwein he yele AWURADE ayɛ kyɛ, “Ngɔto dwein ngɔye AWURADE ayɛ, ofikyɛ wama ye nwo so ngonim nu; wagyi pɔngɔ ne pɔngɔhanɛniɛ ne wagua ɛpo nu.
AWURADE te m’anwoserɛ ne me dwein, na wayɛ me ngoadefoɛ.
Ɔte me Nyameɛ, na ngɔye ye ayɛ, me baba Nyameɛ ɛne, na ngɔma ye so.
AWURADE te koɛhonɛniɛ; ye dumaa li AWURADE.
Ogyili Faro teaseɛnam mɔ ne ye asraafoɛ guale ɛpo nu; na Ɛpo Kɔkorɛ afa ye koɛhonɛfoɛ atitire nemɔ.
Buma ne akata bɛ so, na bamono bahɔ ye bo kyɛ nyɔboɛ.
O AWURADE, wɔ sa famaa ne te ngonim ne tumi, O AWURADE, wɔ sa famaa ne dworɔm pɔfoɛ ne.
Ɛnate wɔ tumi piri ne aso ɛkã bɛ bɔ bɛko betia wɔ ɔ gua; Ɛsoma wɔ yaa piri ne, na ɔyera bɛ kyɛ ngyɛngyɛma.
Wɔ bonyi anu nwomeɛ mane nzue ne boaboale ye noa, asorɔkye ne gyinane berɛ kyɛ ɛwaen; na buma ne bɔle kunguma wɔ ɛpo afia.
Pɔfoɛ ne hane kyɛ, ‘Ngɔpo bɛ so, ngɔɔto bɛ, ngɔhyɛ koɛ nu nzesadeɛ ne, na me kra ko koyi.
Ngɔhwe me ngrandɛ, na me sa kɔma bɛ boso konua.’ Ɛmane wɔ nwomeɛ tuli mvrama, na ɛpo ne fale bɛ; na bɛmonone kyɛ kungumaboɔ wɔ buma ne anu.
O AWURADE, nyameɛ foforɛ nemɔ, bɛ nu nwa yeɛ ɔne wɔ bɛte pɛ ɔ?
Nwa yeɛ ye krongronyɛlɛ totohyia te kyɛ wɔ ɔ, bɔ ye nwo yɛ suro wɔ ngonim nu, ná ɔyɛ anwanwadeɛ kyɛ wɔ ɔ?
Ɛtengyɛle wɔ sa famaa nu, na aseɛ memene bɛ.
Ɛnate w’anwumvoinnwunɛ so ɛyɛle mmenia bɔ ale bɛ ne taataa, na ɛnate w’anwoserɛ so ehyirele bɛ atee maa bɛhɔle nekaa krongron bɔ ɛte ne.
Maen maen ate, na bɛ nwo wosowoso bɛ; na bɛ bɔ bɛte Filistia ne, ahunundetelɛ atɔ bɛ so.
Afei Edom ahemvo mɔ babɔ fuin; ɛserɛ aha Moabo atitirefoɛ; na bɛ bɔ bɛte Kanaan amukoraa b’ahone atu.
Ahunundetelɛ ne ɛserɛ atɔ bɛ so; ɔnate wɔ tumi asaa ne ati, bayɛ dinn kyɛ nyɔboɛ, kɔpem kyɛ, O AWURADE, wɔ mmenia kɔpɛ nu kɔhɔ ɔ, kɔpem kyɛ mmenia bɔ ale bɛ ne kɔpɛ nu kɔhɔ ɔ. Ɛkɔfa bɛ kɔwa, ná aabɔ bɛ atenaseɛ wɔ wɔ bɔbɔ wɔ bokaa ne aso, nekaa bɔ afa ayɛ w’atenaleɛ ne, O AWURADE, nekaa krongron bɔ afa wɔ sa asiesie ne, O AWURADE.
AWURADE koli hene afebɔɔ.” Miriam edwein ne Mmerɛ bɔ Faro mbɔngɔ mɔ, ye teaseɛnam mɔ ne ye pɔngɔhanɛfoɛ hɔle ɛpo ne anu nen, AWURADE mane ɛpo nzue ne sale ye si oobu fale bɛ so; nakoso Yisraelfoɛ de, bɛfale aseɛ wosee so wɔ ɛpo ne afia.
Afei ngɔmhyɛlɛniɛ Miriam bɔ ɔte Aarɔn aliɛma brasua ne, ɔfale akasaa tirale, na mmrasua ne amukoraa bɛwosole akasaa begole abilie befitele belili ye si.
Na Miriam surole so kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔto dwein bɛ́ye AWURADE ayɛ, ofikyɛ wama ye nwo so ngonim nu; wagyi pɔngɔ ne pɔngɔhanɛniɛ ne wagua ɛpo nu.” Mara nzue weewee ne Afei Mose mane Yisraelfoɛ tuli bɛ bo befili Ɛpo Kɔkorɛ ne anwo, na bɛfale bɛ nye behyirele Sure ɛserɛ ne aso.
Bɛnatele ɛserɛ ne aso ɛlɛsa mumua bɔ bannwu nzue ɔ. Na beedwuli Mara nen, bangora Mara nzue ne no, ofikyɛ né ɔyɛ wee.
Yiti bɛfrɛle berɛ Mara.
Na mmenia ne penepenene bɛ komvi beguale Mose so kyɛ, “Nzue beni yeɛ yɛ́nya ye yɛ́no ɔ?” Yiti Mose sũ frɛle AWURADE, na AWURADE hyirele ye bakaa bie.
Ogyili bakaa ne tole nzue ne anu, na nzue ne yɛle fɛ.
AWURADE yɛle ahyɛdeɛ ne nhyehyɛleɛ mane bɛ wɔ berɛ, na osole bɛ neane wɔ berɛ.
Na Mose hane kyɛ, “Sɛ ekotie AWURADE wɔ Nyameɛ dwirɛ, ná ayɔ bɔ ɔsɔ ye nye, ná ali ye mmeraa dwirɛ ne ye ahyɛdeɛ mukoraati so a, ye de anwonyerɛ bɔ nde nguale Misraimfoɛ so ne, mengɔte nu biala ngogua wɔ so; ofikyɛ me ole AWURADE, wɔ safoɛ ne.” Afei beedwuli Elim, nekaa bɔ asue ti buru ne nyɔ ɔne ayee aburasoo wɔ ne, na bɛkyekyele asikyeleɛ wɔ nzue ne noa.
Mana ne nnomaa Yisraelfoɛ tuli bɛ bo befili Elim, na Yisrael ɛlɔen ne amukoraa wale Sin ɛserɛ bɔ ɔla Elim ne Sinai b’afia ne aso.
Betu befili Misraim aseɛ so ne, bosome bɔ ɔtɔ so nyɔ ne anu, kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so buru ne nnu ne aso yeɛ bedwuli Sin ɛserɛ ne aso ɔ. Na Yisrael ɛlɔen ne amukoraa penepenene bɛ komvi beguale Mose ne Aarɔn so wɔ ɛserɛ ne aso.
Besele Mose ne Aarɔn kyɛ, “Sɛ AWURADE tumi maa yɛwuwuli Misraim aseɛ so a, ahaa ɔte paa.
Berɛ de, yɛtenatenane naen kukue nwo yɛdidili yɛtele naen mane yɛ ko yili pambee.
Nakoso ɛmɔafa yɛ baagua ɛserɛ so wa kyɛ bɛbaama ɛhɔen ku maen ye amukoraa.” Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔtie, ngɔma aleɛ kɔtɔ kofi anwuro kogua ase kɔma ɛmɔ.
Ɛlɛho biala mmenia ne kofite kɔɔsesa bɔ ɔkɔso bɛ di sɔ kyẽa ne ɔ. Na ɛhe kɔmaa ngonwu ye sɛ bekoli me mmeraa so anaakyɛ bengoli so a. Na kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so nzia ne, sɛ bɛboaboa bɔ bɛkɔsesa ne noa a, ɔsɛ kyɛ ɔyɛ ɛlɛho biala deɛ bɔ bɛsesa ne ye faa nyɔ.” Yiti Mose ne Aarɔn sele Yisraelfoɛ ne kyɛ, “Ɛnɛ nɔsoa, ɛmɔkonwu ye kyɛ AWURADE yeɛ ɔyele ɛmɔ fili Misraim aseɛ so ɔ. Na ngyerɛmɔ koso ɛmɔkonwu AWURADE animnyam, ofikyɛ AWURADE anwu kyɛ ɛmɔpenepene bɛ komvi begua ye so.
Na yɛ de, yɛ ole nwa bɔ ɛmɔpenepene bɛ komvi begua yɛ so ɔ?” Na Mose sele kyɛ, “Nɔsoa biala, AWURADE kɔma ɛmɔ naen ma ɛmɔkoli, na ngyerɛmɔ koso, ɔkɔma ɛmɔ aleɛ ma ɛmɔ ko koyi; ofikyɛ AWURADE ate kyɛ ɛmɔpenepene bɛ komvi begua ye so.
Na yɛ de, yɛ ole nwa?
Nna yɛ yeɛ ɛmɔpenepene bɛ komvi begua yɛ so ɔ, na mmom AWURADE.” Na Mose sele Aarɔn kyɛ, “Ka kyire Yisrael ɛlɔen ne amukoraa kyɛ, ‘Ɛmɔhwe bepingye AWURADE, ofikyɛ wate kyɛ ɛmɔpenepene bɛ komvi.’ ” Na Aarɔn noa wɔ so bɔ odwudwo kyire Yisrael ɛlɔen nen, bɛtole bɛ nye bɛneane ɛserɛ ne aso dɔ, na mvum nu, AWURADE animnyam yele ye nwo ali wɔ munungum ne anu.
Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Mate Yisraelfoɛ bɛ komvi bɔ bɛpenepene ne.
Yiti ka kyire bɛ kyɛ, ‘Nɔsoa ɛmɔkoli naen, ná ngyerɛmɔ wora ɛmɔali aleɛ ama ɛmɔ ko ayi; amaa ɔnate so ɛmɔanwu kyɛ me ole AWURADE ɛmɔ Nyameɛ ne.’ ” Odwuli nɔsoa ne, ayenzii mɔ tuli bi beeyi bɛfale asikyeleɛ ne; na aleɛ hyene ngyerɛmɔ nen, ɛborɔ guale asikyeleɛ ne anu nekaa biala.
Na ɛborɔ ne yakyili gualɛ nen, mvum nu, nikyee mmaa mmaa taataa bie bɔ ye hatahata te kyɛ asukɔtwea guaguale ɛserɛ ne aso.
Na Yisraelfoɛ nwuni ye sɔ nen, bebisabisale bɛ nwo ngoko ngoko kyɛ, “Nzikyɛ nikyee ɛhe?” Ofikyɛ né bɛnze nikye horɛ.
Na Mose sele bɛ kyɛ, “Aleɛ bɔ AWURADE afa ama ɛmɔ kyɛ ɛmɔli hɔ ɛne.
Bɔ AWURADE ahyɛ hɔ ɛhe: ‘Ɔsɛ kyɛ ebiala sesa somaa bɔ ɔkɔso ye di ɔ; olonka ngoko ngoko.
Ɔsɛ kyɛ ebiala nea mmenia somaa bɔ bɛwɔ ye ɛtena sua nu ɔ ná ɔsesa.’ ” Sɔ ala yeɛ Yisraelfoɛ yɔle ɔ; ebiemɔ sesale pee, yeɛ ebiemɔ wora bɛsesale kãa bie.
Nakoso bɛfale olonka besusuli nen, sona bɔ ɔsesale pee ne deɛ ammo so, yeɛ sona bɔ ɔsesale kãa bie ne koso, ye deɛ wandɔ si.
Ebiala sesale bɔ ɔkɔso ye di ɔ. Yeɛ Mose sele bɛ kyɛ, “Nnɛma ebiala yakyi bie ma aleɛ kye so.” Nakoso bandɛ Mose so.
Ebiemɔ yakyili bie ma aleɛ hyene so, na ngaka wale nu maa ɔbone mvii.
Na Mose fɛle bɛ so yaa.
Ngyerɛmɔ biala, ebiala sesale bɔ ɔkɔso ye di ɔ; nakoso sɛ eyia bɔ a, né wahuro.
Kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so nzia ne, bɛsesale aleɛ ne mmɔhoɛ nyɔ; ebiala sesale olonka nyɔ.
Mbanyi amukoraa bɔ bɛlela ɛlɔen ne noa ne, bɛwale Mose berɛ bɛɛbɔle ye amaneɛ, na Mose buale bɛ kyɛ, “Bɔ AWURADE ahyɛ hɔ ɛne: ‘Ɛhema te nwomelelɛ kyẽa bɔkɔɔ, afofikyẽa krongron ma AWURADE.
Yiti bɔ ɛmɔkɔtoto ne, ɛ́mɔtoto, yeɛ bɔ ɛmɔkɔto ne koso, ɛ́mɔto.
Na bɔ ɔkɔha ne, odi kyɛ ɛmɔfa besie maa odwu ɛhema ngyerɛmɔ.’ ” Yiti bɛfale bie besiele mane aleɛ hyene so, kyɛbɔ Mose ha hyirele bɛ ne; wammo mvii, yeɛ ngaka koso amma nu.
Na Mose sele kyɛ, “Ɛ́mɔli ye ɛnɛ, ofikyɛ ɛnɛ te afofikyẽa ma AWURADE.
Ɛmɔngonwu bie wɔ buro ɛnɛ.
Elesia yeɛ ɛmɔfa bɛsesa ɔ; nakoso kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so nzoo, bɔ ɔte afofikyẽa ne de, ebie ngɔte ngogua.” Kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so nzoo ne, mmenia ne biemɔ hɔle kyɛ bɛkwaapena bie bɛsesa, nakoso bannya bie.
Na AWURADE sele Mose kyɛ, “Kyinzu koraa yeɛ ɛmɔkɔpo me mmeraa dwirɛ ne me mmeraa maa okoodwu ɔ?
Ɛmɔanwu ye kyɛ, AWURADE ama ɛmɔ afofikyẽa, na ye sɔ ati yeɛ kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so nzia ne, ɔma ɛmɔ elenyɔ aleɛ ɔ. Yiti ɔsɛ kyɛ ebiala tena ye awuro; nnɛma ebiala tu ye gya baa fite fi ye awuro kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so nzoo ne.” Yiti mmenia ne lele bɛ nwome kyẽa bɔ ɔtɔ so nzoo ne.
Yisraelfoɛ frɛle aleɛ ne mana.
Né ɔte kyɛ mviɛlɛ, fitaa, na ye fɛɛ te kyɛ apiti bɔ woɛ wɔ nu ɔ. Na Mose sele kyɛ, “Edwirɛ bɔ AWURADE aha ato berɛ hɔ ɛhe: ‘Ɔsɛ kyɛ ɛmɔfa mana olonka ko besie berɛ bɛma ɛmɔ si ama mukoraa bɔ bɛkɔwa ɔ, amaa ɔnate so banwu aleɛ bɔ mva mane ɛmɔ lili wɔ ɛserɛ so, mmerɛ bɔ nyele ɛmɔ mvili Misraim aseɛ so ne.’ ” Na Mose sele Aarɔn kyɛ, “Fa talie, ná fa mana olonka ko gua nu; ná fa sie AWURADE nyunu, maa bɛ́fa bésie wɔ ɛmɔ aworɛ ndoatoasoɛ amukoraa nu.” Na kyɛbɔ AWURADE hyɛle Mose nen, sɔ ala yeɛ Aarɔn fa siele Adanzeɛ ne anu, kyɛ bɛ́fa bésie ɔ. Yisraelfoɛ lili mana afoɛ aburanna, maa oodwuli kyɛ bedwuli aseɛ bɔ mmenia tete so ɔ so; na belili mana toonn kɔpem kyɛ bedwuli Kanaan aseɛ so ɔ.
(Olonka ko te graa ko bɔ bahyɛ nu buru ɔ).
